1)
The Path of the Will
<Prayer> Beloved Father! At this time, we are gathered here at the Gangneung Headquarters with our young children. 
Please be with these children whom you have raised with your concern until now, and grant them your presence, work, and grace at this time. Everything we have longed for and missed has been realized through our relationship centered on you, Father, so we earnestly hope that you will enable us to look up to you more broadly and greatly, putting forth our utmost effort. 
Each of our hearts is anticipating the fulfillment of the will you pursue, so now we must unite centered on this will. Thus, we wish to direct the path that this nation must take in the future and become your children who can live meaningful lives as people on this land, so please allow it. 
At this time, as we have gathered, please personally preside over us and guide us in all things. And there are family members who could not attend here, so we ask that you also protect them with the same grace. I pray all these words in the name of the True Parents. Amen. 
<Words> If there are people here who are seeing the teacher for the first time, please raise your hands. Many of you. 
I don't know how many family members are here. Are all the people here family members? "Yes." Then shall we talk about family members tonight? "Yes." 
You may have a vague understanding of what responsibilities and missions our Unification Church is currently undertaking. Also, when viewed in the context of providential timing, you may not clearly know what limitations we have reached at present and how we should respond and proceed in the future. Based on this premise, I will speak on the topic of "The Path of the Will." 
The Purpose of God's Creation of Humanity
We, the family members, well understand that God has been carrying out the restoration providence until now due to the fall of the human ancestors. What God has been doing until now has been to find the lost children, and it would have been good if this historical process had gone as God intended, but it has not happened as intended repeatedly, resulting in continuous extensions until now. 
Because humanity has become the children of Satan due to the fall, it is not a simple matter for such humanity to return to God's realm of love. It is not that they fell by not keeping a promise, but rather that they fell bloodline-wise, so they cannot return to God's realm of love without correcting the bloodline. Therefore, you must understand that God had to walk the path of labor for thousands of years. 
Originally, when God created Adam and Eve, He created them as children. Even from a common-sense perspective, if God is the main character of love, then that God, who is the main character of love, would want to find an object to love with absolute love, which would not be Himself. This means that one cannot stand in a position to love alone. Since the noun "love" must have an object to exist, even the absolute being cannot love alone. 
In this way, since God cannot love alone, He must create an object that He can love. Therefore, He created all created beings, which were made in His image, and among them, He created humanity to stand in a creative position as beings who could represent His personality. 
Such humanity must have the nature to rejoice when God rejoices and to grieve when God grieves. If one cannot experience and feel God's inner heart, no matter how much God loves humanity, that person cannot stand in a position to harmonize and become one with God. Therefore, when God created humanity, He had to create them in such a way that they could rejoice together and feel that love. Thus, humanity was created to possess values similar to those of the absolute being in order to stand in a relative position to the absolute being. 
God's Love and Human Desire
So, to what extent must God bestow love in order to love humanity? Wouldn't He want to love from the highest position? If the absolute being created only one person, He would love that person from the highest position. 
When we, as humans, receive God's love, what position would we want to receive it from? No one would want to receive God's love from the position of a servant. Even if I ask everyone gathered here today, it would be the same. There is a way to receive God's love from the position of a servant and from the position of a child, but if I ask which position you would prefer, you would dislike the position of a servant and want the position of a child. 
Furthermore, if I ask whether you want to receive love from the position of a child or from the position of a direct descendant, what would you answer? It is an obvious answer. Regardless of who it is, everyone would want to receive God's love from the position of a direct descendant. This is the desire of humanity. 
This desire of humanity is not something that is demanded from an impossible position. The absolute God who created humanity would want to love from the highest position, so He must have created the internal foundation for humanity to receive love from the highest position as well. Therefore, we humans also want to receive love from the highest position and want to love from the highest position. 
What is that highest position from which we want to receive love from God? That position is the position of a son or daughter. Wanting to receive love from such a position is precisely what it means to be human. Thus, it naturally leads to this conclusion. If God also has the heart to love humanity to the fullest, what position would He want to share love from? It is the same as humanity. 
If you were to ask God, "When you created humanity, what position did you intend to love from?" would He answer, "Ah, I created humanity to share love from the position of a servant"? If so, that God would not be the God of absolute love. Would He then answer, "From the position of a child"? That is not it either. Therefore, God cannot help but love humanity from the position of sons and daughters. This position is not something that is unreasonable. 
God has a heavenly standard, and we humans have a human standard. So, when we consider what the point of convergence is where these two can come together, that position is the one that both the absolute God and humanity desire. It is the position where, centered on one parent, sons and daughters can mutually give and receive love. 
God's Relationship with Humanity
If God is the absolute being, how would humanity want to regard Him? He is the most precious being in this world, the one with the most love, and the one most needed by humanity. So, if we ask what kind of relationship humanity wants to establish with such a God, humanity would respond that they want to regard Him as the best being and establish the best relationship with Him. 
In other words, if we ask humanity whether they want to regard Him as their master or as their father, they would say they do not want to regard Him as a master. Anyone would inevitably answer that they want to regard the absolute being as their father if they could. 
For example, if we ask men in South Korea whom they would like to be their father-in-law when they get married, most would unanimously say they want to be the son-in-law of the president. Similarly, if we ask women whom they would like to be their daughter-in-law to, most would say they want to be the daughter-in-law of the president or the king. Why is that? Because the president or king is the highest in the country. Regardless of who it is, humanity aims for such a highest position as their goal. 
Considering this fact, when we ask what kind of relationship humanity wants to maintain with God, they would undoubtedly answer that they want to regard God as their father. Is that right? 
Therefore, whether or not there is religion, if there is a God, what kind of relationship should that God establish with humanity? If that God is the God of absolute love, then He must regard humanity as His children and love them from the position of a parent. This love would undoubtedly be the most wonderful love in the world, taking the best position. 
So, what is the position where human standards and heavenly standards can be grafted together? It is the position of a parent-child relationship. In the relationship between humanity and God, where God is called Father and humanity is called sons and daughters, that is the position. When that happens, the desires of humanity will be fulfilled, and the desires of love will also be fulfilled. Additionally, the desires of heavenly providence will be fulfilled, and the connection of heavenly lineage will also be completed. It must be so. 
I have a dry throat. Since the end of the year, I have spoken a lot, and at the beginning of the year, I have spoken continuously for over ten hours a day, so my throat has become very dry. I know that speaking like this with a dry throat is impolite. However, please understand. 
God has been working through His love to love humanity from the highest perfected position. Based on that foundation, God desires to have people who can bring Him the utmost joy. Such a person, according to the principles of our Unification Church, is called a perfected person. 
In other words, a person who has no blemish in any direction, who is without fault inside and out, is a perfect person who can indeed be revered by all people and also by all heavenly spirits. Furthermore, when God looks at such a person, He can say, "Indeed, it is good." 
When one possesses such value that is not lacking in any way and has a character that can be left for future generations, that person becomes a perfected individual with no shortcomings, and God Himself rejoices when He looks at that person. 
Isn't that true for you as well? Mothers often become enamored when they look at their babies. Aunty, have you all felt that way? When the baby is truly cute and beautiful while sleeping, the mother looking at the sleeping face cannot help but break into a smile. The mother who gazes at that face naturally cannot help but show a joyful expression. 
If the love between fallen human parents and children is like this, how much more so for God when He looks at a perfected person? If there is a true son or daughter among humanity who is without blemish and possesses everything, what would God say when He looks at such a son or daughter? God would say, "At last, I have found the son I have been looking for and the daughter I have been searching for." When He gazes at that son and daughter with joy, what kind of expression would He have? Can you imagine? 
That joyful expression would be incomparable to the joyful expression of parents looking at their child after many generations of being the only son in a precious family. It cannot be compared. 
If God were to have such perfect sons and daughters, He would say, "Ah, this is my love among loves, my bone of bones, and my flesh of flesh." Moreover, He would exclaim, "These are the essence of my marrow and the gathering of my blood, my heart's flower, and my entire hope." If God had such a son, what would it be like? And if He had such a daughter, what would it be like? Surely, God has envisioned such a scenario, hasn't He? 
If God has ever had the experience of loving a perfected son or daughter, 
He endowed humanity with the vitality of life when He created them. Without love, that vitality cannot exist. 
Humanity resembles God and possesses God's vitality and heart. When we consider humanity itself, we must establish a connection with God, and we must ask where the eternal home of love and the origin of life are. That place is not the society we live in today, nor is it the nation of South Korea. 
Today, when we see that humanity carries a deep-seated anxiety and is in a situation where they are trying to escape from their current position, we can understand that the world humanity truly desires is not the society and world we are living in today. This is a fact that everyone knows. 
That is why people do not say this world is a good place to live. 
So, has God ever loved a perfected person?
as that, he would not care about his siblings either. If he is driven by his physical desires, he will only think about satisfying himself, disregarding the feelings of others. This is the nature of a person who is led by their body.

In a situation like this, can that person maintain relationships with others? No, they cannot. They will end up isolated because their selfishness drives everyone away. This is why it is essential for a person to control their body with their mind.

Now, let’s consider the path that a person should take. A person must walk the path of life, and to do so, their body must follow the intentions of their mind. This is the essence of living a conscientious life. When a person is conscientious, their body acts in accordance with their intentions. In other words, when the mind governs and controls the body, the body gradually aligns itself with the mind.

If a person can make this small shift, they can move away from evil. However, if the mind submits to the desires of the body, what happens? They are drawn away from goodness. As they move further away from goodness, they become evil. This is a fundamental truth that you must understand.

Now, where do heaven and hell, good and evil, and the rise and fall of fortunes originate? Do you think God punishes? God does not punish; rather, it is because I am destined to receive punishment that I am punished. It is something I create for myself. Just as it is natural for trees to sprout leaves in spring, if a tree does not produce leaves in spring, it will die. This principle applies to you as well. You must always think from this perspective.

Therefore, one must cut away one of the two—either the mind or the body. The body must be cut away. If one does not cut away the body and allows it to act on its desires, will they prosper or perish? They will perish. You know this well. Why do they perish? Because a person who allows their body to dictate their actions will want to take what belongs to others. If someone has something good, they want it for themselves. If there is something delicious, they want to eat it all. This is the nature of the human body.

Imagine three friends, and one of them cannot control their body and instead follows its desires. Will the other two friends stay by their side? No, they will leave. Therefore, there is no other way but to fail. A person who is led by their body is like a communist, thinking, "What is mine is mine, and what is yours is mine." They claim everything as their own and try to possess everything. In such a case, will the two friends remain by their side, or will they run away? They will run away. 

Let’s say there is a family with ten members, including parents. If one of them is driven by their physical desires, will that person think about their parents at all? They will not consider their parents. Instead, they will rush to eat all the delicious food first. Not only that, but they will also disregard their siblings.
is the path to becoming a central figure. When you sacrifice for your family, your parents become your parents, and your siblings become your siblings. Your parents will say, "I will be your father and mother," and your siblings will say, "We will be your brothers." Do you understand? 

You must clearly understand this. Ultimately, when you engage in sacrificial service, what happens? You become the central figure. Sacrificing for others leads to a situation where you are loved and respected. This is the principle of growth in a family or community. 

When you live for others, you create a bond that strengthens relationships. It is through this selflessness that you build a foundation for a harmonious environment. 

Now, consider this: if you sacrifice for your family, how does that affect your relationships? Your parents and siblings will recognize your efforts, and in turn, they will be more inclined to reciprocate that love and support. 

This is not just a theoretical concept; it is a practical truth that applies to all aspects of life. When you put others before yourself, you cultivate a sense of unity and cooperation. 

In a society where everyone seeks their own comfort, those who choose the path of sacrifice will stand out. They will be the ones who lead by example, inspiring others to follow suit. 

So, as you navigate your own lives, remember the importance of sacrifice and service. It is through these actions that you will find true fulfillment and create a positive impact on those around you. 

In conclusion, the path of sacrifice is not easy, but it is the most rewarding. It is the way to true happiness and the foundation of a strong community. Embrace this principle, and you will grow into the person you are meant to be.
I thought I would disappear and fail, but when I stand in a position where I can gain trust through sacrifice and service, my father and mother will place me in front, and my siblings will also elevate me, making me the center of the family. Do you understand? "Yes." 

Furthermore, even if the parents pass on their inheritance within the family, I want to share everything through you. The siblings will say, "That older brother or younger brother is undoubtedly a reliable person, so we entrust everything to him." Therefore, if one is meek, humble, and engages in sacrificial service, there is ample opportunity to grow as the center of the whole. Do you understand? 

However, if one does not sacrifice or serve at all and instead sacrifices the family for oneself, then not only the father and mother but all the siblings will leave one’s side, and one will become lonely and isolated. If there is anyone who desires to be lonely and isolated, raise your hand. Such a person is bound to fail. Everyone will abandon them. You must clearly understand that becoming lonely and isolated leads to failure. 

An individual should sacrifice for their family; that is the duty and virtue. Moreover, a family should sacrifice for its clan; that is also a virtue. Sacrificing for something greater than oneself is virtuous. For instance, if there is a Kim family in a neighborhood, and one household within that family sacrifices for their clan, then everyone in that household, including the head of the clan, will bow their heads to that household. The people of that household will be welcomed, and they will want to be on the side of that household. The head of the clan will want that household to live beside them. Even the servants will express a wish to work for that household. 

In light of this, is it evil or good to sacrifice one’s family for the sake of one’s tribe? "It is good." You must understand this. 

If there is someone who lives sacrificially for their neighborhood, all the people in that neighborhood will bow their heads to that person who has sacrificed, and they will automatically seek out their embrace. In this way, they can conquer the neighborhood without fighting. They will conquer completely. Then, even if that person does not want it, the neighborhood will say, "You must become the owner of our neighborhood. Please be our center." Is that right or not? "That is right." 

If there is a clan called Kim or Park, that clan must unite as one to sacrifice for the Republic of Korea and save this country. We must understand that it is our clan's duty to sacrifice. 

Only when such sacrifices are made can that clan make the tribe and nation their own. When this happens, that clan can become a central clan that fully inherits the thoughts and spirit of that nation. Furthermore, the entire nation will seek to unite around that clan. Do you understand? Because of such clans, the nation can be formed into a unified entity. 

If the Kim clan sacrifices to save the country, is the motivation for that sacrifice good or evil? Is that sacrifice good or evil? You must understand this well. 

Even if the Republic of Korea were to perish, if all thirty million citizens sacrificed to save the world and create a true, good world, what would the people of the world do? They would connect everything, including the thoughts and history of the Republic of Korea, to themselves. When it is said that the world has been blessed because a nation and a people have sacrificed, will the result of the Republic of Korea’s sacrifice manifest as good or evil? It will manifest as good. Therefore, we must move toward a global era while doing such things today. 

The Difference Between a Great Person and a Saint 

Everyone, there are many great people who have been loyal to their countries in the world. So, are there great people in the Republic of Korea? "Yes." Who was there? "General Yi Sun-sin." He is a great person of the Republic of Korea. However, the Japanese see him as an enemy. This is the problem. 

Loving and serving one’s country is good. However, if the ideology of that country can lead the world and is centered on the world, then that country can become global. Do you understand? And the person who establishes that ideology becomes a hero. That hero can become a hero of the world. 

When we look at today’s great people, there are many who have been loyal only to their countries. However, there is not a single global great person. They may be praised in their own country, but they are seen as enemies in other countries. A person in such a position cannot lead the world, cannot inherit the goodness of the world, and cannot achieve it. This is why we say that saints and great people are different. You must understand this. 

So, who is a saint? A person born in their own country and living as a citizen of that country is not someone who only loves and serves that country. Of course, such a person is a patriot. However, a saint is someone who lives not only for the current country but for the eternal future country, for such a world. Only such a person can participate in the ranks of saints. Do you understand? 

Thus, saints and great people are different. Those attending university can understand this, right? A saint is a global person. However, a great person is a national person. Do you understand? Nowadays, scholars also aspire to become global scholars, right? You must clearly understand this. In other words, a great person loves only their own country, while a saint represents the ideals of the human world. Do you understand? You must clearly understand what the way of a saint is. You must study or ensure that it is firmly lodged in your mind. This may differ slightly from the "path of intention," but it is something you must know. 

When we look at saints, they lived centered on heaven. Teaching only about the human world cannot allow one to participate in the ranks of saints. A saint is someone who resolves all issues centered on heaven as the first principle. They have guided based on the standard of God. In other words, they have unraveled human ethics. 

They did not think of a national perspective for a single country but rather considered a worldview based on a global level. 

God does not seek to save one country but seeks to save the world. Of course, He saves one country to enable that country to save the world. Do you understand? The absolute God seeks to save the world; therefore, unless one teaches the way concerning humanity based on that God, they do not qualify to participate in the ranks of saints. 

When we speak of the four great saints, who are we referring to? Let’s list them. Jesus, Buddha, Confucius, Socrates—are these the four great saints? What about Muhammad? Is Socrates a true saint? No, he is a philosopher. A philosopher is someone who understands all principles through knowledge. Knowledge alone cannot lead to acts of devotion. Did any of Socrates' disciples sacrifice their lives to follow him? You must understand this. 

The way of a saint transcends life. Do you understand? Therefore, it is said to abandon life. One must possess the great authority to abandon this life, which exists in an evil world, and must have the active subjectivity to control their own life force to become a saint. 

Knowledge cannot control life. As mentioned earlier, even if a certain professor has hundreds of doctoral degrees, when their child is born, that child does not inherit the father’s knowledge but inherits the father’s bones and flesh. Is that not so? Knowledge is unrelated to life. Therefore, the seed of knowledge cannot become the true framework or law of human life. 

However, a saint must develop the strength to protect and sustain their life even in the face of death, and they must possess such active power. Only with such a global perspective can one become a saint. In light of this, Muhammad should be considered one of the four great saints rather than Socrates. Do you understand? "Yes." 

A Doctrine Centered on Heaven Must Emerge 

The four cultural realms have emerged centered on the four great saints. There is no cultural realm of Socrates. There are cultural realms centered on Indian culture and Buddhism, the Confucian culture of the Far East, Christian culture, and Islamic culture. Is there a cultural realm of Socrates? No, there is not. These have provided spiritual nourishment to humanity throughout history and have played a leading role in life. However, what is Socrates? He is a philosopher. Therefore, Socrates is not particularly significant. You must understand this fact. 

Thus, a person who teaches a doctrine centered only on humanity cannot participate in the ranks of saints. In other words, they cannot become a saint. A saint is someone who seeks to unify today’s human world with a global ideology centered on God and in place of God. Saints possess such global ideologies and doctrines. It is through these ideologies and doctrines that they can ascend to the position of a saint. Do you understand? 

So, is a saint national or global? "Global." A saint is global and at the same time God-centered. You must understand this. 

Then, why have the religious leaders placed the title of saint upon themselves? They must do so; otherwise, God does not exist. In light of this, my assertion that a comprehensive repair factory and specialized technicians are necessary to solve future human problems is correct. Can one still deny the existence of God? 

Today, what is the standard for establishing the way of ethics? It is based on the teachings of saints, synthesized according to the direction indicated by their ideologies. This is also being practiced as the ideology of the state. Moreover, the world follows the principles of that ideology. Ultimately, what is that ideology centered on? It is centered on God. 

In light of this, the world of unity based on truth must manifest as the world that saints desire. Therefore, if a doctrine centered on heaven does not emerge, it will lead to the conclusion that God cannot exist. Do you understand now? Do you understand or not? "I understand." You must understand this well. 

So, do you want to become a saint or a great person? "I want to become a saint." Everyone has many desires. This is something that does not need to be asked. The ladies and grandmothers here are probably the same. Even though they are older now, everyone wants to become a saint. This is something that does not need to be asked. 

Looking back through history, this is why the founder of the Unification Church, Reverend Moon, has sought to unify the world of religion, revolutionizing humanity to become leading individuals based on the ideals of heavenly fortune. So, does that make you feel good or bad? "Good." The members of the Unification Church may feel good, but those who are here for the first time might feel bad. 

Be a Three-Dimensional Person 

However, even if you feel bad, if you think about it, it is still good to have become a Korean. If you had become a person from another country, wouldn’t that feel worse? Isn’t that right? How would you feel if you had become Japanese? You would feel bad, right? Still, since a Korean has become the leader of the Unification Church, it may feel bad, but it is better than if someone from another country had done it. 

So, how will I make the young people of the Unification Church into global saints? I will make them into people who are even better than saints. What would happen if I were to create people better than saints? Would the Republic of Korea bow its head or not? "It would bow." Would Japan bow its head or not? "It would bow." Would America bow its head or not? "It would bow." Would people of all races bow their heads or not? "They would bow." Even the lowest classes would bow their heads. 

So, what is the best way to make them bow their heads? It is to let love be done according to my will. That is why I have also arranged marriages according to my will. This time, I married about 800 couples. People from America, Japan, England, France, Italy, and about ten other countries came to participate. When I called them, they came well. They cannot help but listen to my words. Therefore, they cannot love without listening to my words. They may not know it, but once they understand the principles of our Unification Church, they will find that they cannot love without listening to my words. That is why they will absolutely listen to me. Is that not so? 

In the future, I plan to build a beautiful tourist hotel in Korea. I hope to build one with about 120 floors. I will become the owner of the most expensive hotel in the world and attract many guests to the hotel. This will help the Republic of Korea prosper. If I can do that, there will be nothing bad for the Republic of Korea. 

If Reverend Moon had been placed in front of the Republic of Korea right after liberation, he would have made the country wealthy and still had more to spare. This is an undeniable statement. However, because the country opposed it and the church opposed it, I was forced to follow like a fool. It was like carrying a sacrificial offering to the top of a mountain and slipping, falling into the valley. We have managed to pull this to the top. We are almost there now, right? 

That is why we must also conduct ideological education for educational officials and ideological education for high-ranking officials. Therefore, in the future, all the training conducted by the Unification Church must be absorbed by the intelligence agency. They would have absorbed and merged the Victory Alliance four or five years ago if it had not been for Reverend Moon of the Unification Church. It is because of Reverend Moon that they could not absorb it. What did I say? Did I ask them to give me food or rice cakes? If they want to do that, they should do it when I am gone. Once people have been educated, they will all choose to follow Reverend Moon of the Unification Church rather than their own affiliations. It is because of this time that they have all been restored. 

I am the leader of the Unification Church. Being a leader does not mean I am someone special. I am not exceptional. I eat three bowls of rice a day; what is different about that? However, there is one thing that is different. What is that difference? It is that my thoughts are different. My ideology is different. My perspective is broader and three-dimensional than yours, but there is nothing else that is different. Do you understand? 

And everything I say turns out to be true. Many years ago, I...
The words I spoke are now perfectly fitting. Even when discussing the current situation, it fits exactly. This is the difference. Therefore, while others may be complicated in their actions, I can simply go over there and wait quietly, and everything will unfold as I envisioned. This is what makes it different. 

Those who know for sure and practice will remain until the end. 

That is why Unification Church members listen closely to the words of Teacher Moon. If you listen to my words, you won't be deceived by others. If you observe the Teacher quietly, there are times he may appear like a fraud. (Laughter) He speaks boldly without any basis and shoots out fear. However, after about ten years, it turns out to be correct. This is why people cannot help but fear the Teacher. South Korea fears him, Japan fears him, and the United States fears him. Isn’t that enough? What’s wrong with that? Isn’t it? Now, I will speak openly about everything. 

To those who are here for the first time, it may be rude, but let’s speak frankly like men. You are men, and I am a man, so let’s have a frank conversation. Is there anyone here who came because they like the Unification Church? Thinking about this makes me feel bad. Some people come thinking, “Listening won’t hurt,” and then they get caught. There may be some of you who are here for the first time. However, what bothers me the most is that there are people who came with the mindset of, “I heard rumors about Teacher Moon of the Unification Church, so let’s check it out tonight.” 

Am I some kind of monkey in a zoo? This really makes me feel bad. 

I am not someone who has to do advertising to survive. Even if I don’t advertise, even if I am stuck deep in the valleys of Geumgangsan, thirty million people will come to me saying, “Please save me.” I am not someone who needs to show myself off to advertise. That is why the Unification Church does not advertise. It’s absurd; why would I need to advertise the Unification Church?

2)
Fundamental Restoration
Mary was not in a position to easily answer the question of whose baby this was. She could not help but say that she was conceived by the Holy Spirit through God's power. When Mary said such a thing, what man would believe that she was conceived by the Holy Spirit? Joseph, having risked his life to save her, must have thought that she was making excuses and lying to hide her true identity from her lifesaver. Due to such circumstances, there must have been an indescribable internal trouble between Mary and Joseph.

The stories surrounding the birth of Jesus, both inside and out
Moreover, the fact that Joseph brought his betrothed without a feast and secretly was bound to attract attention from relatives and townspeople. In such a situation, neighborhood children and friends could not help but look at them with strange eyes.

As time went on, there must have been internal troubles between Joseph and Mary centered around issues they could not understand, and such facts naturally could not help but become rumors.

On January 10, 1971 (Sunday) early morning, at Gangneung Church.
* This message was given during a national district tour, and the earlier part was not recorded. The material (recording tape) was provided by Lee Yu-seon, the head of the Gwanak Church.

When such strange rumors began to circulate, Joseph's relatives and brothers could not help but ask him about them. Likewise, his parents and uncles could not help but inquire about those rumors. Each time, Joseph could not boldly defend himself or Mary, so he could not help but hesitate, and his attitude revealed an air of suspicion. Thus, the rumors spread not only throughout the neighborhood but also to nearby villages.

In such a situation, as a month and two months passed, Mary's belly, which was carrying Jesus, grew, and she found herself in an environment where she could not go outside due to embarrassment. At that time, Mary would have preferred to fly away if she could, or to sink into the ground if that were possible. However, unable to do so, she had to endure the uncomfortable and unbearable days of hiding her body from people's eyes for a period of ten months.

During that time, Mary must have prayed before God. She would have wished to go to a desolate desert or any place where no one knew, to give birth to her child.

If Mary were to give birth in such an environment, in such a town, how much would the rumors have spread? How would Joseph's parents or relatives view it? And if there were grandparents, how would they perceive it? When Mary gave birth, she should have praised with joy, but instead, they would have viewed it suspiciously, making it a problem.

As Mary and Joseph found themselves in such a complex and peculiar environment, the day of delivery drew closer. At that time, a decree was issued by the Roman Emperor for all the people of Judea to register. Thus, while on the way to the City of David (Jerusalem), Mary gave birth in Bethlehem. This is the story surrounding the birth of Jesus. 

Wouldn't any man question the circumstances if his betrothed were to become pregnant? Wouldn't there be issues raised regarding his betrothed's pregnancy? Of course, Joseph...
Because the angel subtly taught me something, I tried to understand it internally, but I must have wanted to know the reason. In the midst of this, Jesus was born on earth. Joseph should have always treated Jesus with joy, but he could not do so. The feelings of a stepfather towards a stepchild are something that those who have not had a stepchild cannot understand.

The sorrowful childhood of Jesus
Joseph, from the perspective of a stepfather, had to deal with Jesus, who was born through his fiancée Mary, and from ten months prior, he had been a source of concern, causing internal struggles between him and Mary. His feelings towards Jesus could not have been good. Of course, he knew he should treat Jesus with joy, thinking of what heaven had taught him, but his physiological emotions took precedence, making it impossible for him to treat Jesus with joy or from a position of delight. This was undoubtedly the position of Joseph, the stepfather.

Jesus had no choice but to grow up in such a twisted triangular relationship. The fact that Jesus, born in Bethlehem, had to grow up in Egypt was partly because King Herod wanted to kill him, but it can also be seen as God's grace, knowing well the circumstances of Jesus, who could not return to his hometown due to such a story.

Thus, even after spending over three years in Egypt, he could not return to his hometown. He grew up in Nazareth by the shores of Galilee. As Jesus matured, he became aware that problems arose between his parents, Mary and Joseph, because of him, and that their home was enveloped in an unpleasant atmosphere. It is reasonable to think that Jesus had to live in such an uncomfortable environment.

For this reason, even when Jesus was cradled in his mother’s lap, he had to be mindful of his stepfather Joseph, and Mary, even while breastfeeding, could not do so with a joyful face. In the presence of Joseph, she had to breastfeed with a sense of shame. You must understand that Jesus grew up in such a triangular relationship.

Although it is not in the Bible, you should know that during the holidays, all the children in the neighborhood wore fine clothes and ate good food, but Jesus always stood in the loneliest position, unable to avoid feeling sorrowful. Mary could not provide better food or care for Jesus than for her other children, and she had to do so while being mindful of Joseph, enduring a lonely trial. Jesus grew up in such a life.

The Bible mentions that when Jesus was twelve years old, Joseph and Mary took him to the Jerusalem temple. In that account, Joseph and Mary left Jesus at the temple and returned to find him three days later. Which parent in the world would leave their twelve-year-old son alone and return? From a common-sense perspective, such a thing could not happen anywhere.

So why did it happen? Even if Joseph did not want to treat Jesus that way, he could not help but regard him as a stepchild. There were always problems because of Jesus.

Mary realized that she had left Jesus at the temple when they went up to Jerusalem. However, she could not ignore Joseph's feelings. If Mary suggested taking Jesus with her while Joseph was sulking, there would be arguments and problems, so she followed along, knowing this. Thus, they returned home, and it was only after three days that they went back to find Jesus. Joseph, upon reflecting, realized that leaving young Jesus alone was something no human could do, so he found himself in a position where he had to go to bring Jesus back.

At that time, Jesus was discussing the scriptures with the priests and scribes in the temple. Seeing this, Mary asked, "Why have you treated us like this?" (Luke 2:48). Jesus replied, "Why were you searching for me? Didn't you know I had to be in my Father's house?" (Luke 2:49). What does this mean? It was a rebuttal to his parents. From the parents' perspective, what could they say after leaving their child alone for three days?

Furthermore, when the disciples told Jesus that his mother and brothers were looking for him, Jesus said, "My mother and brothers are those who hear God's word and put it into practice" (Luke 8:21). Does this mean that the parents acted according to the will of the Father or not? When considering these statements, you must understand that in Joseph's household, Mary could not fulfill God's will centered on Jesus.

Mary's position
After Jesus left home, Mary first met him at a wedding in Cana at a relative's house in Galilee. Jesus, knowing that there was a feast at the relative's house, went there and met Mary. When Mary told Jesus that the wine had run out at the feast, Jesus responded to her, "Woman, why do you involve me?" (John 2:4). You must recognize that within this statement lies a hidden internal story that Jesus could not share with anyone.

What this means is that Jesus had a mother, a grandmother, and in the neighboring village, he had a sister and a younger sister, as well as other male and female relatives. Yet, he had not married by the age of thirty. Wouldn't that be the case? At thirty years old, he was only serving as an apprentice carpenter without any concern for marriage, which means Mary, as a mother, failed in her responsibilities. Regardless of the difficulties, Mary should have guided Jesus on his path and deeply discussed his future, knowing that he would carry the will of heaven. She should have asked, "What path should you take?" and worked together with her son in secret to achieve that will. In this respect, Mary failed to fulfill her responsibility in guiding Jesus on his path.

One thing you must understand here is that without a son who can receive God's love on this fallen earth, a daughter who can be loved by God cannot emerge. This is the principle of creation. God first created Adam, that is, a man. And then, based on the man, he created a woman. Therefore, a son whom God can love must be born on this earth first.

But is there such a son on this earth? There is not. Therefore, God must have a beloved son, and to bring forth such a son on this earth, he must borrow a woman's body. Isn't that so? He must borrow a woman's body.

So what position does Mary hold? She is a servant before God. Mary stood on the side of heaven but was originally a woman born through the lineage of the archangel. The archangel became Satan. Mary was the first woman in the historical era to return to heaven among fallen women.

When the angel Gabriel appeared to Mary and announced, "You will conceive and give birth to a son" (Luke 1:31), Mary replied, "How will this be, since I am a virgin?" (Luke 1:34). The angel responded, "For no word from God will ever fail" (Luke 1:37), and Mary said, "I am the Lord's servant. May your word to me be fulfilled" (Luke 1:38), pledging that if there is a way to fulfill God's will, she would be prepared to face everything with her life on the line. Thus, Mary became the first woman in history to stand for God, prepared to face life and death.

Mary could stand in this position because she transcended issues of face, prestige, and life and death. Without such a resolution, she could not accept it. Even though she was already engaged and in a determined situation, the possibility of such an event would disgrace her family and lower her prestige. Moreover, according to the law of Moses, she would be destined to die. However, knowing that this path was God's will, she accepted it, dedicating everything and preparing for life and death. Consequently, Mary emerged as the first woman in history who could face God's will.

Mary was a servant. She was a servant standing on the side of the archangel, the daughter of the archangel. God had to send His son to this earth, but without a woman, He could not give birth. Therefore, He had no choice but to borrow the body of a woman on the side of Satan to send the holy prince of God. God did not do this out of joy but because without a woman, He could not give birth to a child who could bless this world, so He borrowed the body of a servant to bring Jesus into the world. Do you understand?

Mary is a servant. Mary is not the mother of Jesus. While she stood in the position of Jesus' mother, she was a woman whom God borrowed to give birth to Jesus. Today, it is wrong for the Catholic Church to venerate Mary. It was only because without Mary’s body, the Son of God could not come forth. Isn't that so?

The restoration providence to establish a son on the side of heaven
So who is Jesus? He is instead of Adam. He is the lost Adam. Because Adam fell, Jesus was found to be embraced again within God's love. Therefore, the Jesus who was born this way is different from you. Some may ask how Jesus is different from you and why he becomes the Messiah, and why he becomes the Son of God. Mary is also a fallen descendant who inherited the lineage of Satan. Although Mary came out according to God's will, she was a woman whose body was defiled through the lineage of Satan, so Jesus, born through such a woman, also became a defiled body. Thus, Satan can accuse him.

For this reason, God has been fighting a historical battle to indemnify that. In Adam's family, Cain and Abel fought. These brothers grew up and fought. What was the fight about? It was a struggle to exchange brothers. Ultimately, the elder brother must yield to the younger brother. To explain this in detail would take a lot of time, but I will briefly touch on it.

Children born as the fruit of love have an elder sibling, and then a younger sibling, one, two, three, four, in sequence. Thus, they stand before their parents in a position of servitude. Isn't that so? The fruit of love from one parent stands in a line from one position. If there is an elder sibling, the younger sibling comes sequentially. However, due to Adam's fall, Cain and Abel stood in a horizontal position. Cain and Abel stood in a horizontal position, meaning they stood side by side. The fruit of love became two.

According to the original principle of creation, can the fruit of love become two? The principle is that it should become one fruit, but because it became two, it must establish a condition to stand in the position of one fruit. To do that, how must it be? To be born as the fruit of love on this earth, it must not be born centered on Satan. Isn't that so? Who should it be born centered on? It must first be born centered on God. However, it was first born centered on Satan. Cain, who was born centered on Satan, became the elder brother. It was reversed.

Originally, sons and daughters should have been born through God's love. They should all have become God's children, but the firstborn, Cain, became the son of Satan. Therefore, without establishing everyone in the position of God's sons and daughters, God cannot govern humanity, and humanity cannot live happily with God. However, since it became two branches, this is a serious issue. Therefore, the elder brother on the side of Satan must inevitably yield to the younger brother on the side of heaven.

Why must it be so? From a principled perspective, if Adam and the archangel had not fallen in the Garden of Eden, they would have united centered on God. The three would become one. First, God and Adam must become one, but they could not. Then, Adam and the archangel could not become one, and the archangel could not become one with God. This is the fall.

Because Adam could not become one with God, he could not become God's son, and God also could not possess the factors of complete life and perfect love. Adam established a relationship of life with Satan and loved with Satan instead of connecting with God's love. This is the problem. If Adam had become a son who was eternal in God's life centered on God's love, all problems would have been resolved. If that had happened, Adam would have received God's love, but due to the fall, he lost his position as a child of God. Thus, Adam received the life of Satan and the love of Satan. Isn't that so?

Therefore, in the path of restoration, what must be done first is for Adam to become one with God. They must become one body. Without becoming one body, life cannot be connected. Next, Adam and the archangel, and God and the archangel must become one. This is the principle. The order of life must be connected from God to Adam and from Adam to the archangel. Therefore, God must love Adam, and the archangel must love Adam, but due to the fall, the opposite occurred.

For this reason, to restore this, one must stand in a position of love, so one must yield. Isn't that so? The person in the position of the elder brother must yield to the person in the position of the younger brother, so the history of exchanging the positions of younger and elder brothers has been the history of the restoration providence until now.

The reason we must love our enemies
One thing you must understand is that Satan has been the source of sin until now, and why did Jesus insist that we must love our enemies? 

Originally, Satan was the archangel. However, that archangel said, "I have fallen and become Satan, but since God is the omniscient and omnipotent absolute being, shouldn't He resolve things centered on the laws He established? Even if I have become Satan by breaking the law, God, being the omniscient and omnipotent absolute being, should act according to the laws He set?" Wouldn't that be so?

What is that law? From the time of creation, God established the law that He must love the archangel from the position of completion. Therefore, even after completion, He must love the archangel. Isn't that so? However, at the level of completion, the archangel fell. At the level of completion, both humans and the archangel fell. However, because God established the law that He must love the archangel at the level of completion, the archangel, despite having fallen, insists that God must love him once from the position of completion; otherwise, He cannot appear as the complete God.
In the end, Satan is saying, "Your will cannot be fulfilled unless you set the condition that you loved me once at the place of completion you have achieved." Do you understand what that means? 
Next, it revolves around humans. Since God is omniscient and omnipotent, if the Son of God has been completed, then His will is fulfilled. Therefore, Satan, claiming that the completed son who has gone to the place of completion is "Your son and the one who will inherit Your achievements," asks, "Has your son ever loved me as a completed son?" This is where the two conditions come into play. That is why it has taken 6,000 years. 
God is in the place of completion, but the day God meets the completed day is the day humans are completed. With the completion of humans, God appears in the place of completion. Therefore, if Jesus, sent in place of Adam, stands in the completed position and can inherit this whole, then God's completion begins. This is both God's completion and human completion. 
That is why God cannot expel Satan without entering into the heart of the completed human son and establishing the condition that He loved Satan through that son. Knowing this situation, Jesus understood that God had walked the path of suffering for 4,000 years because He could not resolve this one standard of completion, and He was in a position where He had to resolve this grievance, even if it meant walking the path of death on the cross. Is that right? 
That is why Jesus prayed for His enemies, saying, "Father, forgive them, for they do not know what they are doing." (Luke 23:34) Even towards the enemies who killed Him, even in the position where His life was taken away, Jesus had no choice but to pray for His enemies with a heart of love. This is what it means to have loved, not to have punished. He established the condition of having loved. 
Thus, God can say to Satan, "My son loved you even in the position of death. He loved you even in the position of sacrificing His life, so did He not show the greatest love in love? Although you fell from the position of the archangel and became Satan, did He not do what a master can do for you, who originally held the position of the archangel? Is there not enough love of completion with the authority of God's son?" At that moment, Satan cannot help but answer, "Yes." Do you understand? 
So, "Originally, humans are completed sons, so you, who are Satan, must love him and absolutely obey him, and you must love him as much as you love your own body. Love him." This means total submission. Satan retreats here. Therefore, when you love God more than Satan and love Jesus more than Satan, Satan cannot touch you. Thus, from here, Satan is separated from the Kingdom of Heaven, that is, from paradise. Do you understand what I mean?

Additionally, the teacher loves those who can do this in place of the nation. When standing in a position to love one person in place of the nation, to love in place of the entire Christianity, and to love in place of the entire family, all grievances of not being able to love the nation, the church, and the family can be resolved. Thus, it is possible to resolve even with these three people. Will it be resolved or not? "It will be resolved." This is not a game.

Next, what is the grievance of Israel? It is the grievance of not being able to serve the sons and daughters of Jesus. It is also the grievance of not being able to serve the couple of Jesus. Resolving these grievances is the essence of the True Parents' ideology. Isn't that right? Have you ever heard Jesus referred to as uncle or aunt? If the teacher cannot be an uncle or a grandfather, then it is a failure.

Now that the teacher can also be a brother and a grandfather, what will happen to the grievances of humanity? "They will be resolved." Therefore, there is a place where the grievances of the three generations that could not be resolved in the nation, church, and family can be resolved. Originally, what was the center around which grievances began to accumulate? It began centered around the family. The extension of the family is the church, and the extension of the church is the nation. Ultimately, where is the starting point of grievances? The family. Jesus also chose Peter, James, and John, who represented three families, but because they could not unite, they could not fulfill the will. What do these three represent? They represent all of humanity, the church, and the family. They also represent three sons and daughters. They represent everything. However, because they could not unite, grievances were accumulated, and thus they must unite to resolve them.

To resolve these grievances, what was not loved must be loved, and what was not received must be received. However, even if the teacher does this, what should you do among yourselves? This is the problem.

Centered on Jesus, there should have been Jesus' grandfather, uncle, older brother, younger sister, and younger brother. This situation must be recreated. This is the family and the clan. Do you understand? Therefore, this is a microcosm of the nation, the church, the clan, and the family. It all comes together.

For this reason, older grandfathers must become the real grandfathers of Jesus. They must love Jesus from the perspective of being a grandfather. In doing so, the grievances of not being able to love Jesus from the grandfather's position must be resolved. Therefore, we must love Jesus. Thus, those who are of an age to be grandfathers should treat the young men of the Unification Church as if they were young Jesus. By thinking of that young man as Jesus and loving him, the grievances of the grandfather who could not love Jesus must be resolved.

The same applies to those who are of the age of uncles. When has a relative of Jesus, an uncle, ever loved Jesus? Without loving Jesus, one cannot enter the kingdom of heaven. Just as it is said, "I am the way, the truth, and the life; no one comes to the Father except through me," one cannot go to heaven without loving Jesus. Because the uncle of Jesus did not love Him during Jesus' time, today, in the Unification Church, those in the position of an uncle must love the young man as if he were Jesus, thus resolving the grievances of the uncle who could not love Jesus.

The same must be done by grandmothers and aunts. Also, those who are of the age of older brothers or sisters must think of someone among the Unification Church members as their younger sibling, not as a younger sibling but as Jesus. If they have such a thought, no matter how young they are, can they say, "Hey! Listen to me!"? When standing in the position of an older brother or sister in front of someone who is like a younger sibling, they must treat that young person with the care they would give to Jesus. In doing so, they must resolve the grievances of not being able to love Jesus as an older brother or sister.

Jesus also had younger siblings. Because they could not love Jesus as their older brother, that must be restored. This is what you are to do here. What has arisen to do such things? It is the family. Centered on whom? "On Jesus." If you cannot love in such a way, you cannot go to heaven.

Therefore, Unification Church members receive love from others in place of Jesus. They are to receive love in place of Jesus. The older grandfathers are the same. Everyone must love and receive love in that way. Women should also love and receive love with the heart of being Jesus' wife. Do you understand what I mean? The place where this happens is heaven.

What is the Fall? It is being expelled from the realm of God's love. Then what is heaven? It is the world where God's love is realized. What, then, is God's desire? It is for the nation, the church, and the family to love Jesus. Jesus' desire is to receive such love and then to serve God closely, loving grandfathers, uncles, aunts, older brothers, sisters, and younger siblings. Therefore, our entire family must be able to embrace Jesus. If, in the midst of that, a son or daughter of Jesus is born, we should be able to celebrate, saying, "What a great blessing for our family!" By loving in this way, we must be able to resolve the grievances of the three generations. The privileged foundation that can resolve those grievances is the family spoken of in the Unification Church. It is from that family that we say to start everything, which is why Unification Church members are called family. Thus, you are gathered as those who will love each other as family. Do you understand?

Therefore, we Unification Church members must love each other more than brothers, and be closer than parents centered on parents. Can such a game be played or not? If it cannot be played, then you must pack your bags and go find such a place. If you can build such a relationship, then the kingdom of heaven will be realized from here.

With such a heart, transcending borders and races, if you can adapt and realize this wherever you go, that place will be heaven. That is why we call Americans and Japanese all family. Because we can love and like each other like relatives, international marriages are not a problem. Our young men and women should marry black people as well. Their faces may be black, but they are your older brothers and sisters.

When we look at dogs, there are various types like black dogs, yellow dogs, and spotted dogs, but they all give birth to puppies together. Is there a principle that black ones should only live with black ones? All are people created by God, so should we discriminate against them just because we dislike black skin?

If the entire humanity can love each other in a unified relationship across borders and races, and if they stand in a position to love and be loved by the prince of heaven, that is heaven. Heaven is realized from such a place.

Therefore, you must train yourself to love your family and love the 30 million people of South Korea and humanity. You must receive love from the nation and be loved before all of humanity. Only then will the will be fulfilled. Therefore, you must make it possible to receive love. To do so, you must share blessings. When you give and receive love, that place transforms into heaven.

We do not conquer the world with weapons. We build a unified world with love. The ultimate method to conquer the world is nothing but love. When we embrace the world with love, will heaven be realized or not? Thus, we must fulfill the mission of Jesus. Therefore, we must resolve the grievances that Jesus could not resolve, the grievances that God could not resolve, and at the same time, we must be able to resolve the grievances that humanity could not resolve. Those who have resolved grievances will surely be thanked by God. God could not say, "Thank you for resolving my grievances" on behalf of Jesus. Thus, as we resolve the grievances that have been historically accumulated, we will inherit and fulfill the mission of Jesus. When that happens, we will have the authority to say that we are better than Jesus. And we will go to the kingdom of heaven with dignity and without shame.

Love one another.
When we look at Jesus, the three sons of faith, that is, the three disciples, drove Jesus away. Consequently, the twelve disciples drove Jesus away, and the seventy disciples drove Him away, and the one hundred twenty disciples drove Him away. So how many people should you evangelize? You must evangelize as many as one hundred twenty people and send them off to marry. Do you understand? "Yes." Since the teacher did it, you must do it too.

Do you now understand how heaven is realized? How is heaven realized? By applying the principle of Cain and Abel, separating the archangel, and then becoming the sons and daughters of one brother and one parent, one must become a person who receives love from the parents. To do this, we must love each other just as Jesus did. By doing so, heaven will be realized. This is the essence of establishing heaven. Those who have gone out to evangelize should not be eating properly while those who remain eat well. The teacher is resolving the grievances of Jesus, resolving the grievances of God, and resolving the grievances of humanity, and you must also achieve the process of fulfilling the earthly purpose, God's purpose, and humanity's purpose. In doing so, you will be able to say that you are better than Jesus and become the sons and daughters of God. For this purpose, I hope you will make every effort with your utmost sincerity. Do you understand? "Yes."

Did you not have breakfast? What time should we depart? I have spoken a lot today. You are blessed to be sitting here listening to such profound secrets of heaven. <Words> Among those gathered here this evening, those who are seeing the Teacher for the first time, please raise your hands. There may be some among those who have come for the first time who do not practice any religion. Therefore, if we speak only from the perspective of Unification Church members, those who are new may not understand well.
