So tonight, I will first speak a little for the newcomers and then talk about our Unification Church members.

The Difficulty of the Preacher

What is the hardest thing for a person? It is speaking in front of people like this. There are nearly 300 people gathered here, and when I speak in front of these 300 people, everyone pays attention. Each person, whether they are A, B, or C, or if they are Mr. Kim or Mr. Park, all listen and judge according to their own perspectives. Therefore, it is truly difficult for someone to speak in front of many people.

Moreover, if I speak only to the young people, it would be disrespectful to the older ones. Young people need stimulating and explosive actions, so I must speak in a stimulating way to them, while older people require calm content, so I must speak quietly, which creates a mismatch.

Even when singing, the songs that older people like, those that young people like, and those that educated people like are all different.

If I focus on women, it becomes a question of which group of women I should address. When speaking to young people, I cannot just say, "Did that happen? Did this happen?" Sometimes I must say, "Yeah, that's right! That's right!" If I do that, it would be disrespectful to the audience. However, I cannot tell older people that what I said to young people might be a bit excessive, so please understand.

Just like when a locomotive runs, if something trivial is in front, it pushes forward, similarly, when I stand here to speak, if there is an important matter to resolve, I have no choice but to speak that way. If I look at this and that, nothing will be accomplished. You must understand that.

Also, when I talk about men, women should not doze off. Today, you in the Suwon district are the hosts, and I am the guest. Is that right? "Yes." Is that true or not? "It is true." The host must treat the guest well to receive blessings. Do you understand? "Yes." To treat the guest well, one must first be polite. To be polite, of course, one should not be noisy. One must be calm.

When you listen to the words, you should feel as if you are sitting in a spring garden, happily humming a tune, immersed in nature, singing flower songs and butterfly songs, feeling very cheerful. At the same time, your eyes should sparkle with hope. I like that. Do you dislike that? "No, we like it." Some people might not feel that way. Anyway, I hope you treat the guests well today.

If a guest leaves feeling bad, then that household will not be at ease. However, when I say to treat the guest well, I do not mean to bring out a lavish feast. I simply mean to entrust your eyes, ears, and facial expressions to me.

If someone is dozing off in the middle or talking to the person next to them, I cannot just ignore that as the speaker. It would be disrespectful, but I would ask such a person to sit at the back. Even if it is someone who came for the first time, if I see such a person, I would confront them. Would it be disrespectful to say this in advance? Please understand and listen well.

Now that we have all gathered here, we are like close relatives, and if we have a connection, we can connect more closely than anyone else. There may be age differences or gender differences, but this evening, I will speak beyond those positions.

However, one unpleasant thing is that when I see the Unification Church's Teacher, members of established churches glare at me. That makes me feel bad. Yes, I am the Unification Church's Teacher. Some of you may think that the Unification Church's Teacher refers to himself as a teacher, and you might wonder where that kind of talk comes from, but it is polite to elevate one's title. Do you understand? "Yes."

I am the man who has appeared here as the Unification Church's Teacher. I am robust and weigh about 96 kilograms. Some might say, "Unification Church members are thin, but that guy is the leader, so he eats well and is robust." But please do not say that without knowing anything. I do not actually eat well. I have become robust because of my naturally good constitution. So there is no need to say such things.

Now, regarding what I am going to talk about today, I can say good things and bad things. I can also give praise and criticism. Please understand that. Now, shall we start discussing what I want to talk about? "Yes."

The Biggest Problem for Us

When I speak, I dislike taking notes like pastors do, presenting a title and going through it step by step. I am a free person. I can speak as you ask me to. However, since there are many newcomers today, I will set a title and speak. I will speak on the topic of "The Path of Life." This topic is quite broad.

Does the term life include only men, excluding women? "It includes both men and women." Then, should we mention men first or women first? "Men." I asked the men, and that answer is incorrect. Should we mention women first or men first? "Men." Right, that kind of answer should come out.

If we count the people who can cause many problems in the world, would there be more men or women? "Men." There are more men. That makes sense. Now, among those who live with tears in the world, would there be more men or women? "Women." Is that so? (Laughter) Then, among those who like to dance and have fun, would there be more men or women? "Men." It is hard to distinguish. If there are more women, then there are more women, and if there are more men, then there are more men. That is how it goes.

So, when we look at the issue of the path of life today, should we start with women or men? "Men." You say men are the subject? (Laughter) Let’s not hold back and speak freely.

Today, many robust men have come here, and those who believe in the Unification Church will likely accept the existence of God as a given. Have those who do not believe checked whether God exists or not? "I came to find out." They have not checked. If there were no God, what would happen? "Well..." (Laughter)

Today, the biggest issue for us is what life is. This question has been discussed through philosophy, religion, and thought, but still, no definite answer has been given, and it continues to flow along with history. In that sense, when this person, the Unification Church's Teacher, speaks on the topic of "The Path of Life," it is a grand and tremendous matter.

Is There a God or Not?

Now, when we think about whether God exists or not, would it be good if He exists or good if He does not? "It would be good if He exists." When asked to Unification Church members, they would say it would be good if He exists, but what would the communists say? "They would say it would be good if He does not exist." They do not say it would be good if He does not exist; they think He does not exist. In other words, they believe that God is dead.

The question of whether God exists or not is complex. If there is a God, that is, if God were visible to your eyes and anyone could see and meet Him, would that feel good or bad? "Bad." Why is that bad? God is an absolute being, the only one at the very top. Humans want to monopolize such a God, but if everyone could see Him, what would happen?

In this light, if God were among us now, would there be anyone who does not like Him? "No." If such a God were to create humans, would He create men first or women first? "Men first." Is that so?

When it comes to eating good food, should women eat first or should men eat first? "Men should eat first." Women saying that men should eat first is because they have to, but in their hearts, they want to eat first, right? (Laughter) In their hearts, they want to eat first. They have learned that men should eat first, so they have no choice but to let men eat first.

Let’s think about ordinary women. From the perspective of a single woman, men are annoying, flirtatious, and troublesome. If you ask such women, "Should women eat first or should men eat first?" they would say women should eat first.

However, God loves both men and women. Would such a God dislike grandmothers and grandfathers? "No, He loves them all." What about our boys and girls? "He loves them all." Everyone loves Him. But if everyone loves the one God, would there be competition? "Yes." If competition arises, then the strongest person would monopolize God. (Laughter) If that happens, gang leaders or wrestling champions would make God their own. Have you thought about that?

And when we look at the world, would America like God or not? "They would like Him." Would the communist country of the Soviet Union like God or not? "They would like Him." So, would countries fight to seize God? "Yes." They would fight with atomic bombs. Who would stop such fights? Who would stop this fight?

If a handsome God were before our eyes, people would fight to possess Him. This fight would not be the same issue as wars today. A very fierce battle would break out. Have you thought about that? There would be a fierce war to possess God.

Do you think God has thought about such things? Even if I were God, I would think it would be a big problem to appear as a handsome man before people. That is why the absolute God, being deep in thought, remains invisible. This is ideal. Think quietly about it. The fact that He is invisible is ideal.

God Must Be formless

If God were visible, would I be criticized or not? If a visible God said, "Teacher Moon is the real one," would I be criticized? "No." If God were visible and did this, Unification Church members would have already succeeded globally. But because God is not visible, I am criticized, and the Unification Church is criticized. Is this good or bad? Even though I am criticized, it is good. Even if I am criticized, when people realize that the Unification Church is real, those who criticized will want to hide in a mouse hole. (Laughter) So, it is good.

When someone has something precious, what do they do? Do they carry it on their head and like to advertise it? In England, the crown has a 17-carat diamond on it. If you had that, would you walk around London saying, "This is the world's best 17-carat diamond"? "No." Then what should you do? "You should hide it." Where should you hide it? "You bring it home and hide it." Would that make you feel safe? "No." Then where should you hide it? "In the deepest place." Where is the deepest place? "In the heart." Where is the heart? Even if you say you hide it in the heart, you would not feel safe. That is also not safe.

You know how the mind and body fight, right? They fight, and do you know which one is the thief? The mind wants to have it, and the body wants to have it. So, you must ask the diamond where it wants to be kept. If you ask the diamond, "Where would you like to be stored?" what would it say? "In the heart." Why is that? It seems the diamond knows that the heart is a little better. Two thieves...
It seems that among the bunch, there are some who are a little better at heart.

156   The Path of Life
Let’s say there is a treasure in the world that is one of a kind, and on the day it is lost, the world turns upside down. Would you place such a precious thing in the deepest part of your heart, at the very center of your heart? Where would you hide that precious treasure? You would hide it right in the center. Even then, you wouldn’t feel secure and would wrap it up and hide it even more. And who would like to come in and take a look at it? Wouldn’t they dislike it? “They would dislike it.” You would cover it up and wrap it up so that absolutely no one else could see it. This is what people’s hearts desire.

If God were to be seen, would diamonds be the issue in this universe? The absolute being, the unique and unparalleled existence in the cosmos, the absolute being of infinite value, the absolute being of infinite life, if such a precious being exists that cannot be expressed in words, where would you want to hide Him? “I want to hide Him in my heart.” If you hide Him in your heart, would your heart know everything? So, wouldn’t you want to hide Him in a place where no one knows, a place that no one could figure out even after thousands or tens of thousands of years of research? Wouldn’t you want to hide Him? Answer me. “I want to hide Him.” You all resemble me. (Laughter) It can’t be helped.

So, did God do well to remain unseen, or did He do poorly? “He did well to remain unseen.” You said God did well to remain unseen, right? “Yes.” Why? Because there are many thieves. (Laughter) If there were many true people instead of thieves, could they see God or not? “They could see Him.” They could see Him. However, there are no true people in the world. With all due respect, even the older and respectable people here may seem like true people, but they are not true people. If you want to curse me for saying that true people cannot be found, go ahead and curse me. You are not true people.

But what about Reverend Moon of the Unification Church? This is something we need to think about. (Laughter) Let’s talk openly like this. If we speak in a holy manner, it can feel awkward, and we might end up laughing. Since it’s our first meeting, it’s good to open our mouths and laugh heartily and talk. So, let’s get to know each other tonight.

I think it was good that God the Father remained unseen. What do you all think? “We think so.” Therefore, God cannot help but think like Reverend Moon. The conclusion is that it was good that God became unseen. So, God would say, “I have decided to remain unseen.” Do you have any complaints about this? “No, we don’t.” Why should He remain unseen? Because there are many villains.

If they knew God existed, wouldn’t the villains try to find Him by drilling holes in every warehouse? If precious items come into customs, the villains do all sorts of things to find them, so if they knew God existed, wouldn’t they do all sorts of things? God would have to run away. (Laughter) Having said this, we can conclude that it was good that God remained unseen.

The heart that exists but is not seen
However, I want to know whether God exists or not. Can we not know whether He exists or not? Do you know whether there is air or not? “We know.” How do you know? “Because we breathe.” Is there a taste to the air? “No, there isn’t.” You know there is air even though it has no taste.

Similarly, is there a heart or not? “There is.” Where is the heart? “It is not visible, but it exists.” It exists even though it is not visible? “Yes.” With just that, I cannot believe it, but still, it exists? “Yes.” Anyone who says that the heart does not exist because it is not visible is a mad person. I am not a mad person, so I believe that the heart exists.

Then where does that heart come from? “I don’t know.” When a fly lands on your hand, do you have a heart that knows it is there or not? “I have.” When a flea is tickling your hand, do you have a heart that knows the flea is there or not? “I have.” At that moment, the heart is aware of the area where the flea is passing. (Laughter) I don’t know how this heart looks, but it exists. It may seem like there is no heart, but it exists.

I don’t know how the heart looks, but it is truly amazing. Let’s say brothers are having fun together, and their mother comes back from the market with some good snacks and shares them with the older brother and younger brother. The older brother eats everything, while the younger brother saves some and hides the snack bag to eat later. Then, at night, he falls asleep. The older brother wakes up in the early morning needing to urinate, and after urinating, he wants to go back to sleep, but he remembers the snacks the younger brother hid. What happens in his heart at that moment if he wants to eat them? He thinks, “That guy!” Right? No matter how quietly he tries to do it in the middle of the night, he can’t. The heart is the most meticulous supervisor among supervisors.

Does the heart know how to sleep? “I don’t know.” When the body wakes up from sleep, does the heart also open its eyes and follow? When the body’s movements change even slightly, the heart says, “You rascal.” Is that right or not? “That’s right.” This is really strange. Seeing this, we can know that the heart exists. Can you believe that the unseen heart tells the visible body what to do? “I can believe it.” You can believe it because you have a heart, right? “Yes.”

Then where did the heart come from? Think about it. You might be hearing this question for the first time. Let’s assume that there is a God; based on the facts that have appeared, all of nature began with force. However, force manifests itself through action. When force acts, if we analyze that force itself, we can see that it cannot generate force alone. For example, when a wrestler fights to win a championship, can he generate force by himself? He needs an opponent to generate force. There is absolutely no way for force to arise alone.

The conditions for the action of force
So, what must come before force manifests? An opponent must exist before force appears. The absolute condition for the existence of force is that there must be a relative condition. This relative condition refers to the subject and the object. There must be both a subject and an object. In other words, if the subject and object do not interact, force will never arise.

However, the action of this force requires a dual purpose between the subject and the object. When there is a subject and an object, there are the purposes of the subject and the purpose of the object, which means there is a dual purpose. The action occurs when the purposes of the subject and object combine so that neither side suffers loss; when there is loss, no action occurs.

For example, did you come to the Unification Church tonight to gain something or to suffer loss? “We came to gain something.” Let’s think in terms of business. Did you come to gain something or to suffer loss? “We came to gain something.” Whether you came to see Reverend Moon or whatever, the purpose of coming to the Unification Church is clear.

If you came today to gain ten thousand won, but you gained fifty thousand won, you would come again even if I told you not to come. Would you come or not? “We would come.” However, if you came to gain ten thousand won and didn’t gain that much, would you come again if I told you to? You wouldn’t come. Everything is like that. Therefore, no action occurs in a place where there is loss. This is a heavenly principle, a heavenly principle.

If you go to a place like Myeongdong shopping center, you will see many merchants coming and going from early morning. If a merchant goes out in the morning saying, “Today, I’m going out to suffer loss,” would his wife say, “Hurry back”? (Laughter) She wouldn’t say that. The reality of few true people
There are countless people living in the world. However, when we think about how many of these countless people can be regarded as true people worthy of respect from the past to the present and into the future, we see that there are not many who can be called true people.

Among the members gathered here, there may be some who think, "I am a true person who is not ashamed wherever I go." However, truth cannot be twofold; it is ultimately one and only one. In the true sense, a true person is someone who, among the countless humans living in the world, can be considered true only when they measure themselves against a true person. Without a true person who can serve as a standard, this world cannot become a true world.

Then, did the ancestors of humanity not come into existence in a position where they could not become true people? This is something we cannot say. If there is an absolute being who created the universe, namely God, then He must be a true being. This is because He alone is the absolute being, thus absolutely true. Only then can all life and all content belonging to Him be true.

For Him, love must be true love, the mind must be true mind, and the origin of life must be a true origin. Therefore, if all beings that began from such a true source cannot be true, we come to think that the one who created them is not a true absolute being either. From this perspective, if the absolute being who created the world wishes to welcome the highest true human, then our human ancestors must stand in that position.

If our human ancestors had stood in that position, all people living on this earth would have been born as true descendants. However, in the world where humans live today, especially here in Yeosu, can anyone confidently declare, "I am a true person"? This is the problem. If there is a true human among humanity, then the God who created heaven and earth would also desire that human. The issue is why, despite the God who created heaven and earth desiring a true human, there are no true humans on this earth.

Throughout history, countless sages have come and gone. When we look at the teachings of these sages, we see that one taught this way and another taught that way. Among these sages, if there is one whom God would recognize as a true person who can represent humanity in the past, present, and future, who would that be? Humanity does not even know who that person is. Yet, based on the teachings of these sages, humanity has established moral principles and formed the foundations of society and nations. We can see that history has developed in this way. That is why our families, societies, and nations have not yet been able to clarify what is true.

So, when we think about what the true path of life is, we cannot seek the path of a true person without identifying who that true person is.

Humans wishing to relate to the highest being
When we think about ourselves, every person, regardless of who they are, desires greatness and high aspirations. Even our young ladies wish to become wonderful mothers and excellent wives in the future. Young men also wish to become great husbands and fathers.

When we consider how far this standard of greatness goes, it is infinitely high. If you ask a young lady or a young man, "If you were to marry, what kind of partner would you want?" they would answer that they want to marry the best partner in their country. Even boys who know nothing always wish for the best. This is the latent desire within humans.

In this way, if there is the most precious person in South Korea, people want to connect with that person. If there is someone even higher and more precious, they want to connect with that person. For example, if there is a world-renowned president, they want to connect with that president. If a man, he would want to marry his daughter and become his son-in-law; if a woman, she would want to marry his son and become his daughter-in-law. This desire for the highest is common to all.

If there is someone even higher than that, they want to connect with that person. They want to keep climbing higher. When we consider God, there is a position where humans can relate to God, where heart and mind can become one. In that position, all humans, regardless of gender or age, want to relate to God from a close position.

Whether it is possible for us humans or not, our hearts all desire that. Whether small or large, old or young, Korean or American, all humans wish for that.

If that possibility did not exist, how could we humans wish for it? This is the problem. The reason we can wish for it is that there is a possibility. Because there is a possibility, the hope exists in the hearts of all people. If there were no possibility, this longing would not exist.
It is seen as nothing more than a useless mental drain for us humans. Therefore, if there is an absolute being, that absolute being cannot help but instill suffering in humans in order to establish any relationship with them. This is because, without suffering, one cannot form a relationship with the absolute being. If a life can be said to have value in establishing a relationship with the absolute being, it is a life that longs for the highest standard, wants to run towards it, desires to become one with it, and wishes to live together with it. Without this kind of emotional action, humans cannot establish a relationship with the absolute being.

Even the absolute God can only enjoy joy when there is a counterpart. God is the absolute being and the one and only. However, no matter how high He may be, if He is alone, can there be joy or fun? It is worth considering that being alone is not enjoyable. There is no absolute joy in being alone. For example, let’s say there is a world-renowned legal scholar or a person who possesses all the power in the world and can turn the world upside down. Would such a person feel joy just by being alone? No matter how high their position is, there is nothing to be joyful about. If someone were to laugh alone all day long, what would we say about that person? No matter how great that person is, if they are laughing alone, what would we call them? We would say, "They are crazy." 

However, if that person has something small in the palm of their hand and looks at it while laughing heartily, what would we say then? Would we say they are crazy? No one would say that person is crazy. If they hang a painting they created on the wall and express joy while looking at it, no one would say they are mad. Or if they look at a world map and say, "Oh, the Atlantic has grown a bit. The Pacific has shrunk a bit. Korea has become a bit distorted. It has risen too much," expressing their myriad feelings, would anyone call them crazy? No, they would not.

From this, we can see that all the joy and happiness in reality is useless without a counterpart. Joy must come from a counterpart. Therefore, even if God exists, if that God is alone in the highest position with no one around, there can be no joy. Wouldn't that be so?

The same goes for you. Even if you have the confidence to speak in your town and everyone, regardless of age or gender, responds with "Yes, yes," it is of no use when you are alone. No matter how confident you appear alone in a room, that value does not manifest. Even if someone is very confident, when they are alone in a room, they are nothing. No matter how great they may be, they cannot say, "I am the greatest" while being alone.

One must go through a relative environment for the proportions of high and low to be divided; when alone, one is nothing. If someone is alone and boasts about themselves, they are like a monkey. Ultimately, a person gains joy through a counterpart; they cannot find joy alone. Therefore, a counterpart is absolutely necessary.

From this perspective, God is no different. Even the absolute God finds no fun when there is no counterpart. Here, there are elderly gentlemen present, but let’s say an elderly man has lived happily with his wife until she passed away. When a young man thinks about the elderly man, he might think, "What fun could it be to live with an old man? It would just be taking care of him." If the young man greets the elderly man by saying, "Hello! You must be at peace since your wife has passed away," how would the elderly man feel? Would he think, "Wow! You understand my situation well"? No, he would not. This is because the young man does not truly understand the situation of someone living alone. No matter how old a man is, there is no elderly man who enjoys being alone. Likewise, there is absolutely no elderly woman who enjoys living in solitude. When we observe those who live alone in the neighborhood and listen to their words, they often say that living alone is not good, indicating that living alone is not preferable.

Thus, joy springs from establishing reciprocal relationships with one another. In this light, the absolute God is the same. Therefore, God cannot help but create all things to find a counterpart that He can see and enjoy.

Humans are the greatest masterpiece among God's creations. When God created all things, He created humans last. He must have built up from the smallest things to create the most precise and high-level human. No matter how small the creation, would God have created it while crying and feeling sad? Absolutely not. Even when creating the smallest things, He created them with joy.

When you write, even if you put a dot, depending on your mindset at that moment, you can feel joy. That single dot can also symbolize hope. Therefore, even if God created the smallest objects, those creations serve to fill God's lonely position and bring Him joy, making them the highest objects of joy before God and fulfilling the requirements of loyalty and duty. From this, we can understand that God, after creating all things, created humans last. When God created humans, He found that humans are wonderfully made. Humans are indeed wonderfully made. 

How many people are there in Yeosu City? About 100,000? "There are 120,000." Just in Yeosu City alone, there are 120,000 people, so how many must there be in the entire Korean Peninsula? There are nearly 40 million living on the Korean Peninsula. That is not a small number.

God made humans as the most valuable and precise masterpiece. This was not for God to play with humans as toys. When a person creates something, even if they can create it again, they always want to keep the one they put their utmost effort into. Everyone dislikes having that touched. Therefore, when they meet the person they love the most or the object they cherish the most, they want to give it away. Isn't that the nature of our hearts? The reason humans have such hearts is that they resemble the owner who created them. 

When artists paint, even if they paint the same picture, the differences in the personalities of the artists manifest in the artwork. Even if many people paint the same person's face, the personality of the artist is reflected in the painting. Similarly, when you write, even if everyone writes on the same topic, each of the millions of people expresses their own nature in their writing.

Therefore, what does the artwork resemble? It resembles its creator. This is something we already know. So, when we ask whose likeness humans ultimately bear, it is undoubtedly that of the owner, just as children resemble their fathers. 

From this perspective, when we see that we humans like the best and the most precious things, it follows that the absolute being who created us would also like the best. For example, when deciding which of two things is the best, the absolute being would choose the one that is well-made, valuable, and matches His character in every way. Even if there are many objects, people cherish the most valuable among them.

So, what is the most precious creation among those made by God? If there were no absolute being, we would not know, but since there is one, and because of that, there is a created existence, what could be the most precious? The most precious thing is what the owner always wants to keep close and always wants to see. If the owner lives for a thousand years, they would want that existence to be by their side for a thousand years, and if they live forever, they would want it to be by their side forever. This is the desire of our human hearts.

Humans are beings that pursue eternal life. Today, every country has national treasures. When these treasures can represent the culture of that country and symbolize the national character, they become historical relics. The more an object symbolizes the entire nation, the more it remains as a treasure of that country. That treasure is something the country wants to preserve for a thousand years. They manage it to ensure it lasts. Similarly, if there is an owner who created the most precious thing, that owner would love it deeply and want to keep it safe.

From that standpoint, if humans stand at the highest rank among the creations of God, and if the absolute God lives eternally, then humans must also live eternally. Wouldn't that be so? Humans are the most precious beings made with utmost care by the absolute being, and they always wish to gain their desires through Him and to find joy with Him. If people think this way, it is certain that God cannot think otherwise.

If God created humans to be beings that would only exist for a few days and then disappear, then God is not an absolute being. He created them as precious beings that He would want to see forever. If humans are such beings that can bring joy to God, and if God is eternal, then humans must also be eternal. Therefore, the eternal God must be relating to an eternal world. Can this be expressed in words?

However, many people think, "If I live for 70 or 80 years, that's enough; if I die, that's the end," and they consider death as the final point. Yet, those who reflect deeply through the course of history ponder how humans can live without dying and whether there is a way to live longer. The more determined a person is, the more they ask, "What is life? Why do humans come and go like travelers?" They say, "Life is suffering," or "Life is like dew on grass," but if they could live forever, they would not need to worry about such things.

Each of you has a heart that contemplates life. However, if humans are not worthless beings that briefly exist and disappear, but rather beings of infinite and noble value created by the absolute being, then humans are undoubtedly beings that can be with the absolute being. Therefore, it follows that humans must be able to live eternally. When we think about what God would like the most among all the creations in this world, no matter how we choose, there is nothing other than humans. Isn't that right?

The closest beings to humans are said to be monkeys. However, those monkeys simply eat, sleep, and reproduce. They do not know what eternal life is or who God is. They do not long for their hometown, miss their parents, or yearn for sibling affection. Even if they are higher animals, do they think about who God is? Therefore, there is no worship of God, nor any religious practices centered around praising Him in specific places. When we see this, it becomes clear that since humans are the highest among all creations, God still has hope for humans and expects what they will do. Isn't that so?

What is a true person? This becomes the question. No matter how precious a treasure may be, if there is no owner to recognize it, it becomes worthless. However, even the most trivial thing gains value when it is needed by an owner. Isn't that so?

So, what is a true life? You must understand that a life that has lost its owner cannot be a true life. Even objects cannot be true objects if they lose their owner. If there is an object, only an expert who knows its content well or someone who can analyze and manage it perfectly can recognize its value. No matter how many outsiders there are who do not know its content, they cannot understand its value. Isn't that right?

For example, even if there is a diamond, it must be recognized for its value for it to be considered precious. However, there are more fake diamonds than real ones. Real diamonds can cut gold, but fake diamonds cannot. When we see this, we cannot help but think about how value is determined and where noble value is revealed. Noble value is revealed by the owner who seeks and desires it.

Even if the object one possesses seems insignificant, when it becomes one with them deeply, when all its content resembles them to the point where they cannot be separated, they feel infinite value for it, and that value grows even more.

Children are the same. Parents love their children who resemble them more. Do you think that's true? Among children, there are those who resemble their mothers and those who resemble their fathers. Of course, parents love all their children, but they still love those who resemble them more. Parents often talk about which child resembles whom. The father might say, "That child resembles me," while the mother might disagree and say, "That child looks just like me. No matter how you look at it, they resemble me." Yet, the father insists that the child resembles him.

What does resemblance mean? It means having the same nature. Having the same nature means that they can completely become one. This is not temporary; it is a relationship that can be eternally united, and the proportions of good and bad are determined by that relationship. Therefore, they know that they resemble each other.

In the same way, if there is an object created based on the nature and content of the absolute God, which resembles that nature greatly, then the absolute God loves that object. Therefore, the more it is separated, the more it is pulled away, the more it is divided, the more it becomes sorrow rather than joy. When one works, there is a consumption of energy. Isn't that so? Let's take a motor as an example. The power that comes into a motor and the power that goes out are different. When it operates, the energy is consumed, so the outgoing power must be less. The incoming power is always greater than the outgoing power. Isn't that so? When it operates, it must decrease. If a 100-volt light bulb receives 100 volts of electricity and lights up, the power is consumed, and it becomes less than 100 volts. Because of the consumption that occurs during operation, the outgoing power must decrease.

However, there is one thing that can disregard this operation in the universe. That is love. What happens with love? When the power of ten comes in, it comes out with a little more than ten. If true love is given to any object, the power of that love does not diminish but remains forever. Therefore, humans can only find eternal life through the law of love; without love, there is consumption. Do you understand? You must know this.

From this principle, the statement that all things in this world evolved and developed is incorrect. There is no principle that the power entering increases because some powers combine and act. For something new and higher to emerge, a third power must come in.

When discussing mutations and such today, that is incorrect. However, love, the more it is given, does not come out diminished; rather, it comes out increased. **The Way of the Saint**

334   참다운 인생길  
여러분이 그런 사랑을 체험하면 여자들은 시집가지 않으려 하고, 남자들 은 장가가지 않으려고 할 것입니다. 그 사랑에 취하면 아편이 문제가 아닙니다. 술이 문제가 아니라구요. 시골 양반들은 뚝배기에다 탁주 같은 것을 꿀꺼떡 꿀꺼떡 마시고 취하는데, 그런 것에 취해 살게 되어 있지 않습니다. 사람은 사랑에 취해 살게 되어 있는 것입니다. 알겠어요? 여러분이 그것만 알게 되면 사랑을 위해 가는 길이 고생스럽더라도 고생이 아니라는 것입니다. 자기가 사랑하는 사람을 위해서 정성을 들이고 들이고 또 들이는 것은 자랑이요, 영광인 것입니다. 부모가 사랑하는 자식을 위해 뼛골이 녹아나도록 고생을 하지만 힘든 줄을 모르는 것입니다. 왜? 사랑하기 때문입니다. 자기의 피살을 깎아 주고 그 값어치가 얼마인지 장부에 치부해 둡니까? 안 하지요. 오히려 몽땅 주지 못해서 안타까워하는 것입니다. 여기 아주머니들도 그렇지요? 아이에게 젖을 먹이는데 먹지 않으면 왜 안 먹느냐고 안타까워합니다. 그것이 사실은 호스를 갖다 대고 자기의 피와 살을 뽑아 가는 것이 아닙니까? 어떻게 보면 도둑 중에서 최고의 도둑이 아니에요? 그래도 어머니는 아이가 젖을 안 먹으면 안타까워하는 것입니다. 왜 그렇게도 좋아하느냐? 사랑의 법도이기 때문입니다. 그래서 사랑하지 않고서는 영생할 수 없습니다. 그래서 하나님을 사랑이라고 하는 것입니다. 알겠어요? 이런 것을 여러분이 참고해서 알아야 되겠습니다. 원숭이 새끼라고 했다가는 봐라, 이 녀석들. (웃음)  
이게 뭐예요? 마산의 유명한 산물이에요? 이거 선생님 혓바닥이 두꺼워 져서 얘기하겠어요? 감이에요? 여기 지구장은 참 지혜가 많은 사람입니다. 선생님이 너무 늦게까지 얘기하지 말고 적당히 하라고 이걸 가져온 것 같 은데…. (웃음) 선생님이 돌아다녀 본 중에서 제일 지혜가 밝구만. 말보다 실적에서 말이에요. (감을 드심) 대번에 기분이 이상하구만. 왜 그런지 알겠어요? 떫은 감이에요, 떫은 감. (웃음)  
하나님이 인간을 창조하신 이유  
335  
이제 다시 돌아가서, 참사람을 만나 봅시다. 참사람을 만나 보자구요. ‘참사람은 얼굴이 잘생겨야 된다.’ 그 말이 맞아요, 틀려요?「틀립니다.」그렇지도 않다는 것입니다. 또 ‘키가 평균 이상 적당히 커야 한다.’ 맞아요, 틀려요? 「틀립니다.」 ‘참사람은 불구자여서는 안 된다.’ 이거 맞았어요, 틀렸어요? 그런 한계선이 있어요, 없어요?「없습니다.」 참사람이라는 표준 아래서 인간 차별이 있어요, 없어요? 없다는 겁니다. 팔 하나가 없고 다리 하나가 없는 사람이 참사람이 될 수 있어요, 없어요? 몸뚱이만 남은 사람이 참사람이 될 수 있어요, 없어요?「있습니다.」 그런 사람은 무슨 사람이 되겠어요? 무슨 사람은 무슨 사람이에요? 정신 사람이지. 그렇지 않아요? 그러면 절대자가 있다면 그 절대자가 제일 좋아하는 사람이 참사람일까요, 아닐까요?「참사람입니다.」 그것만은 틀림없을 것입니다. 절대자가 제일 좋아하는 사람은 참사람입니다.  
여러분은 하나님의 종이 되겠어요, 양자나 양녀가 되겠어요?「양자나 양녀요.」 그러면 하나님의 친아들딸이 되겠어요, 양자나 양녀가 되겠어요?「아들딸이요.」 여러분이 이걸 생각해야 됩니다. 사람의 최고 희망의 기준 혹은 목적점은 어디냐 하면, 그것은 하나님의 자녀가 되는 것입니다. 그렇지요? 하나님이 절대자이신데, 그분이 인간을 필요해서 지었겠어요, 아니면 필요 없는데 지었겠어요?「필요해서 지었습니다.」 그러면 무엇 하기 위해서 지었겠습니까? 지어 놓고 울기 위해서 지었겠어요, 좋아하기 위해서 지었겠어요?「좋아하기 위해서요.」 좋아하기 위해서 지었습니다. 그렇다면 하나님은 피조만물이 없이 혼자 있는 것을 좋아하시겠어요, 나빠하시겠어요?「나빠하십니다.」 아무리 절대자라고 해도 고독단신이라면 소용이 없는 것입니다. 혼자서 뭐 하겠어요? 혼자서 무슨 재미가 있겠어요? 아무리 한 나라의 대통령이라 해도 혼자 방안에 앉아 ‘아이구 좋아라, 아이구 좋아라’ 하면 뭘 해요? 그러면 뭐 했다고 말합니까? ‘기분 좋아하는 구만.’ 그래요? ‘미쳤다’ 하든가 ‘돌았다’고 하지요? (웃음) 그러나 조그만 아들 사진이라도 들여다보면서 ‘아이구 참 좋다.’고 하면 돌았다고 해요, 안 돌았다고 해요?「안 돌았다고 합니다.」 왜 안 돌았다고 해요? 「아들 사진 보고 좋아하기 때문입니다.」 그러니까 지극히 작은 것이라도 상대적 조건이 있어서 그걸 보면서 좋아하는 것은 천지이치에 들어맞는 것입니다. 상대 없이 좋아할 수 있어요?「없습니다.」 상대 없이 좋아하니까 미쳤다 고 하지. 그것은 있으나마나입니다. 그렇지요? 그러니까 하나님도 좋아하시기 위해서는 상대를 만들어야 되겠어요, 안 만들어야 되겠어요? 「만들어야 됩니다.」 오늘 여기에 기성교회 목사들이 와서 들으면 좋겠구만. 잘 들어 봐요. ‘하나님은 절대자이시며 전지전능하신 분이기 때문에, 죄악된 인간과는 하등의 관계가 없이 거룩한 분이시기 때문에 언제나 기쁘고 영광된 자리에 있나니라.’ 기성교회에서는 이렇게 믿고 있습니다. 잘못 믿는 것입니다.  
하나님에게 상대가 없으면 외롭겠지요, 안 외롭겠어요?「외롭습니다.」 사람은 어떤 주인이 만든 걸작품이지요?「예.」 그 걸작품은 주인을 닮지요?「예.」 닮는다는 것입니다. 그럼 하나님이 사람을 지었다면 사람은 누구를 닮은 거예요?「하나님이요.」 하나님을 닮았다는 것입니다. 사람을 중심삼고 볼 때 하나님은 누구를 닮았어요? 사람 닮지. 그런 것도 몰라요? 아들을 중심삼고 볼 때 아버지는 누구를 닮아요?「아들요.」 아들을 닮는 것입니다. 또 아버지를 중심삼고 볼 때 아들은 누구를 닮아요?「아버지요.」아버지를 닮는 것입니다. 그러니까 하나님은 결국 나를 닮았다는 것입니다.  
하나님은 누구를 닮았다구요?「인간을 닮았습니다.」 인간이라는 그런 것은 다 빼고 나를 갖다 붙여야 좋지 않아요? 그러면 하나님을 삼촌 하나님 만들래요, 내 하나님 만들래요?「내 하나님요.」 남편 하나님 만들래요, 내 하나님 만들래요?「내 하나님요.」 내 하나님이니까 내가 제일 가깝다는 거예요. 내 하나님이라구요.  
이거 운반이 빈번하구만요. 왜 자꾸 그러는 거냐구요? 안 갖다 놓으면 안 먹는 거라구요. 물을 자꾸 갖다 놓으니 쏟아질까 봐 마시다가 보니 다 마셨구만. (웃음)  
하나님께서 천지만물 가운데 원숭이를 제일 고귀한 동물이라고 생각할까요, 아니면 사람을 제일 흥미진진하게 바라보겠습니까? 생각해 보세요?「사람입니다.」 사람이 틀림없습니다. 아무리 훑어봐도 사람밖에 없다는 것입니다. 그러면 하나님이 왜 인간을 좋아하려고 하겠어요?「자식이기 때문입니다.」자식은 나중이고, 결국은 같이 있고 싶어서 그런 것입니다. 같이만 있으면 되겠어요? 같이 살면서 싸움하려고 그러겠어요, 사랑하려고 그러겠어요?「사랑하려고요.」 결국은 좋아하려고 그러는 것입니다. 재미를 보겠다는 것입니다. 재미를 보려면 사람이 없어 가지고 됩니까, 안 됩니까?「안 됩니다.」  
인간의 최고의 소망  
하나님께서는 사람을 사랑하고 사람들도 최고의 높은 자리에 계시는 분, 즉 하나님을 만나려고 합니다. 하나님이 있다면 전부 다 하나님을 자기 것으로 만들고 싶어하지요? 하나님이 우리를 만나려면 어떠한 자리에서 만나고자 하시겠습니까? 하나님은 우리를 어디서 만나려고 하겠느냐? 이것을 알아야 됩니다. 도대체 그 자리가 어디냐? 그 위치가 어디냐? 그 내용은 뭐냐? 이게 문제입니다. 어떠한 자리에서 만나고 싶어하겠습니까? 최고의 자리입니다. 인간으로서도 최고의 자리요. 하나님으로서도 최고의 자리예요, 최하의 자리예요? 하나님도 최고의 자리에서 만나려고 하신다는 겁니다.  
그러면 하나님과 사람이 만날 수 있는 그 최고의 자리가 어디냐? 이것을 인간에게 물어본다면, 인간에게 있어서 최고의 소원이 뭐냐고 하면 하나님의 아들딸이 되는 것이라고 말할 것입니다. 그렇게 되면 하나님은 인간을 대하여 아들딸로 사랑해야 되겠어요, 안 해야 되겠어요?「사랑해야 됩니다.」 인간을 아들딸로 사랑하면 하나님은 인간의 아버지가 되는 것입니다. 자연히 그 자리에 올라가는 것입니다. 인간이 하나님의 아들딸이 되어서 하나님의 사랑을 받게 되면 어떻게 됩니까? 한번 부자의 사랑의 인연을 맺게 되면 떼어놓을 수 있어요?「없습니다.」 사랑하는 아들이 있다면 그 아들을 뗄 수 있어요?「없습니다.」  
사랑하는 아들이 되려면 어떻게 해야 되느냐? 생명의 인연이 일치가 되어야 합니다. 그것이 필요합니다. 본래 사람은 하나님으로부터 태어났기 때문에 하나님의 생명을 받아 가지고 장성하여 하나님의 사랑을 중심삼고 하나님의 아들의 자리에 서게 되어 있었습니다. 그런데 타락함으로 말미암아 생명줄이 끊어졌습니다. 생명줄이 끊어졌기 때문에 사랑줄도 끊어진 것입니다.  
그렇기 때문에 인간의 최고의 소망이 무엇이냐 하면 하나님의 아들딸이 되는 것이요, 하나님의 소망은 우리 인간의 부모가 되는 것입니다. 인간이 하나님의 아들이 되어 가지고 가만히 살펴보니 아버지의 자리가 자기 자리보다 더 낫다고 할 경우에 그 아버지의 자리를 자기 것으로 만들고 싶겠어요, 안 만들고 싶겠어요? 아들이 가만히 보니까 아버지가 자기보다 나은 것을 가지고 있을 때, 아들이 그것을 갖고 싶겠어요, 안 갖고 싶겠어요?「갖고 싶겠습니다.」  
아버지로부터 사랑을 받지만 언제나 아들의 자리에서만 사랑받게 된다 고 하면, 다시 말해서 아버지는 한 단계 높고 나는 낮은 자리에 머물러 있 어야 한다면 기분이 좋겠어요, 나쁘겠어요?「나쁘겠습니다.」 좋지 않겠지 요?「예.」아버지는 아예 윗 자리에만 있고 아들은 아들의 자리에만 있으 면 기분이 좋지 않다는 것입니다. 그러면 기분이 안 나쁘려면 어떻게 해야 되겠어요? 아버지와 한 자리에 설 수 있다면 아들이 좋아하겠어요, 안 좋 아하겠어요? 「좋아하겠습니다.」 좋아한다는 거예요. 그러니 여기까지 올라가야 하는 것입니다.  
하나님을 누구로 삼으려고 하느냐? 하나님을 안고 나와 안팎 관계를 만 들자는 것입니다. 여러분은 이것을 알아야 합니다. 사람의 욕망을 놓고 볼 때 하나님을 어디에 두어야 좋아하겠습니까? 아버지를 중심삼아 가지고는 상하관계입니다. 그렇지요? 그런데 인간은 이것 가지고는 만족을 안 한다는 것입니다. 상하관계도 맺지만 이것은 하나님보다 한 급 낮기 때문에 기 분이 나쁘다는 것입니다. 권세가 하나님에게 있다는 것입니다. 그렇지요? 그러니 기분 나쁘다는 것입니다. 그래서 하나님을 중심삼고 좌우관계, 전후관계, 내외관계까지 갖추려고 한다는 것입니다. 그 자리까지 가려고 한 다는 것입니다.  
인간은 하나님의 몸  
내외관계는 무엇이냐? 하나님을 우리의 몸과 마음을 중심삼고 분석하게 된다면 하나님은 마음 하나님이요, 사람은 몸 하나님이라는 것입니다. 여 기까지 나가자는 것입니다. 이것이 서로 서로 내외적으로 되어 있지만, 내 적인 것과 외적인 것을 두고 볼 때 내적인 것이 낫고 외적인 것이 못하지 않느냐 하게 되면 또 문제가 됩니다. 그렇기 때문에 내적인 것과 외적인 것이 하나되어야 한다는 것입니다. 또 상하도 하나되어야 한다는 것입니다. 그러므로 여기에서 사랑으로 엉클어져야 되는 것입니다.  
안팎이 서로 사랑했다 할 때는 높고 낮음이 있어요?「없습니다.」 또 부 모와 아들딸이 하나가 되면 여기에 높고 낮음이 있어요?「없습니다.」 횡 적인 일체, 종적인 일체가 이루어지는 것입니다. 그럼으로 말미암아 여기 서부터 사랑의 핵심이 이루어져 우주로 벌어져 나간다는 것입니다. 이것이 안 됐다는 것입니다.  
그러면 본래 사람이 어디까지 올라가야 하느냐? 본래 하나님은 인간을 종이 아닌 아들딸로서 지으셨고 하나님의 몸으로 지었다는 것입니다. 알겠어요? 인간 조상이 하나님의 몸이라는 것입니다. 그리고 하나님은 내적인 입장에서 주인이 되는 것입니다.  
여러분은 이 세상 천지에서 가장 귀한 것이 있다면 그것을 어디에 갖다 두고 싶습니까? 남이 모르는 곳에 숨겨 두고 싶지요? 가장 귀한 보물을 가 족다면 남이 잘 보는 길가에다가 매달아 두겠어요? 땅을 파서 묻든가 아무 도 모르는 깊은 곳에 간직하고 싶을 것입니다. 그래요, 안 그래요? 「그렇습니다.」  
그러면 그 보물을 감출 곳이 어디입니까? 지갑이나 몸뚱이에는 둘 데가 없습니다. 감출 곳이 있다면 나만이 알 수 있는 곳, 내 마음 깊은 곳에 갖다 두고 싶어할 것입니다. 하나님도 그것을 원하시겠지요? 그러므로 인간 에서 가장 귀한 우주의 중심인 하나님을 저 우주에 갖다 둬선 안 된다는 것입니다. 하나님을 저 하늘나라에 두면 되겠습니까? 하나님이 이런 것을 아셨기 때문에 인간의 마음 제일 깊은 곳에 계시려고 했다는 것입 니다.  
그러므로 ‘내 마음, 나’라는 것은 자기만이 알지요? 자기만이 관리할 수 있고 자기만이 관계를 가질 수 있습니다. 그렇지요? 여기에 비로소 하나님 께서 안식하실 수 있다는 것입니다. 누가 빼내 갈 수 있어요?「없습니다.」 그러기에 하나님은 어디에 계시려고 하느냐? 우주에 계시려고 하지 않는 겁니다. 재미가 없다는 것입니다. 하나님은 우리의 마음속에 들어와 계시겠다는 것입니다. 그러니까 ‘나’는 행복한 존재인 것입니다. 천하에 이 이상 가치 있는 것이 없습니다.  
내 마음 가운데 들어와 계시는 하나님과 내가 사랑으로 하나되면 나는 무엇이겠습니까? 아들이라면 하나님의 아들이고, 아내라면 하나님의 아내입니다.  
하나님과 내가 주고받아서 하나만 되는 날에는 그도 나요, 나도 그라는 것입니다. 그렇기 때문에 요한복음 14장 20절에 ‘그날에는 내가 아버지 안에 너희가 내 안에 내가 너희 안에 있는 것을 너희가 알리라.’는 말씀을 하신 것입니다. 이 말씀은 하나님과 나는 하나라는 것입니다. 이와 같이 고 귀한 것이 인생입니다. 오늘날 기독교가 이것을 모르고 있습니다.  
사람은 무엇이냐면, 실체를 쓴 하나님의 몸입니다. 하나님의 실체를 쓴 몸이기에 인간은 외적 하나님이라는 말입니다. 알겠어요? 지금까지 종교사 에 그러한 사상들이 있었지만 그 내용은 확실히 밝히지 못했습니다.  
석가는 ‘천상천하유아독존’이란 말을 했지만, 안팎의 사연을 망각하고 신 이 있는 것을 부정해 버리고 자기 자체가 그렇다고 하는 것은 큰 망각이라 는 것입니다. 천도교에서는 ‘인내천(人乃天)’을 말하고 있지만 그것도 마찬가지입니다. 그러므로 사람 자체를 위주로 할 것이 아니라 신과 사람이 합 해 가지고 ‘신을 위주한 사람’인 것을 확실히 규명해야만 천지의 문제가 풀 리는 것입니다.  
하나님께서는 그런 것에까지 우리 인간에게 특권을 부여하려고 하십니 다. 왜? 우리 인간을 사랑하시기 때문입니다. 여러분도 사랑할 때는 다 주 고 싶지요? 내 것을 모두 사랑하는 사람에게 보관하고 싶은 겁니다. 그런 데 그것을 숨기고 싶다면 거짓 사랑입니다. 그렇기 때문에 하나님께서는 모든 권세를 누구에게 갖다 주시려고 한다고요?「인간에게요.」 그렇다면 인간은 모든 전체를 누구에게…. 「하나님에게.」 이렇게 되기 위해서는 사랑으로 하나되어야 하는 것입니다. 그렇기 때문에 창조이상은 무엇이냐? 일체이상입니다. 사랑을 중심삼은 일체이상이라는 것을 여러분이 알아야 되겠습니다.

인간은 영생의 존재  
그러면 오늘날 이 땅 위에서 제일 참다운 사람이 어떤 사람이냐? 하나 님과 안팎으로 한몸이 되어 가지고 자녀 입장에서 완전히 사랑받을 수 있 는 사람이 참다운 사람입니다. 그러한 사람들이 하나님과 함께 살아가는 생활을 참다운 인생길이라고 하는 것입니다. 여러분은 이것을 확실히 알아야 되겠습니다.  
사람들은 어느 누구를 막론하고 최고를 바라고 있습니다. 인간이 최고의 자리에 가게 되면 하나님은 내 것이요, 남의 것이요?「내 것입니다.」 또 나는 하나님의 것이에요, 아니에요?「하나님의 것입니다.」 그렇게 되면 나는 하나님의 아들이 되고, 하나님 자신도 되니, 우주는 누구의 것이 되 는 것입니까?「내 것이 됩니다.」  
그러면 하나님께서 제일 사랑하고 제일 귀하게 여기는 물건이 있다면 그것을 하루, 혹은 10년이나 100년쯤 같이 지낸 후에 집어던지게끔 지었
Would God have created us to be together forever? "He created us to be together forever." It is meant for us to be together eternally. The same goes for humans. Wouldn't it be nice if a person could just be born and die without any further obligation? Do we need to live forever? "We need to live forever." It is essential to live forever. Why? Because the Absolute God, centered on absolute love, needs an object to love. If one could love for a day or two, or even for 10 or 100 years, and then discard that love, that would not be true love. The more you love, the more you want to be together. There are those who have lived as singles, holding onto their deceased wife's handkerchief, right? "No." Therefore, it is a principle that humans must live forever. To live forever, one must stand on a foundation where a stronger force can be exerted. So, do you desire eternal life or not? "We desire it." Even if vaguely, you are hoping for eternal life. (Recording briefly interrupted)

Are there many people in the world or few? "There are many." There are many, but Koreans will become their teachers. If that happens, there will be a teacher-student relationship, but can a student, no matter how talented, take the teacher's place? (Laughter) I am doing this work to make you all into teachers.

For you to become that way, you must understand both inside and out what religion is and what our Unification Church is. When you know this clearly and go out, whether you meet pastors or Taoists, you will be clear. Will there be problems when you meet them? "No, there will not be." There will be no problems. I want to make you experts and turn you into teachers. Then can you always be teachers? By making you teachers and teaching them, if there are many teachers, then the next step is to manage them on a tour. At that time, you will be flying around saying, "Oh, how nice." (Laughter) This is not a laughing matter.

Those who first come to the Unification Church may wonder what Reverend Moon has that is so significant. It may seem like there is nothing, but there is something powerful. Isn't that right? "Yes." The members in Japan will do anything if the leader gives a command. They move even more than the communists. Members in America, Germany, and Europe also move hundreds of times stronger than the commands of their presidents when the leader gives a command.

Will the world become one or not? "It will become one." Our 777 families have many relatives around the world, right? "Yes." In the future, when you board an airplane, you will say, "777, that's three seven." (Laughter) This is good for heaven, good for earth, and good for people. This is about living together.

The Unification Church aims to create a regeneration factory that allows people to walk the path of true life, which is the ideal, and to live eternally within the realm of God's love, creating a happier group of people. This is Reverend Moon's wish for the Unification Church. Those who agree with this, please raise your hands. Put them down. If anyone feels uncomfortable with what the leader is saying, then I feel uncomfortable. Those who feel uncomfortable have not suffered as much as the leader and do not understand religious issues as well as the leader does. If I were to unpack the vast content of the spiritual world, everyone would be overwhelmed. Therefore, you must learn humbly. You must understand what that means.

To repair, one must disassemble oneself. 

That is why the Unification Church is becoming an issue now. If you become a member of the Unification Church and cannot find a place to stand, it will be a big problem. Therefore, you must diligently establish your own place. There is no one more shameful than someone who has no place to stand. If you are invited somewhere and feel good, saying, "Thank you for inviting me on such a glorious day," but then find there is no place to sit, what will happen? You cannot run away, nor can you die. Therefore, you must establish your place.

Establishing a place is not something someone else will clean for you. Such a thing can absolutely not happen in the Unification Church. You must establish your place by yourself. That is the way of principle and the way of restoration, and you must clearly know that you must pave that path.

Now you understand what the true path of life is, right? You must become a true person, but do you know what kind of person a true person is? Knowing that, once you believe, you must not change for your entire life. You must not be swayed by your environment or let your environment dominate you; rather, you must say, "I am the one who dominates the environment, and the environment is dominated by me." You must be certain of this.

And you have learned about the repair factory, right? Then how many methods are there for repairing in this repair factory? The methods of repair are simple. The first is heart repair, and the second is body repair. These two methods are different. The body and heart are similar at a 5 to 5 ratio, which is why they fight. However, if the heart is at 5 and the body is at 1, will the body follow the heart or not? It will follow, right? "Yes." Therefore, what religion does is completely restrain the body. It is about completely breaking down what the body wants. Religion teaches such laws. Thus, religion must always restrain the body.

You are now in the repair factory. If you have entered the repair factory, you must quickly begin the disassembly work. You must take things apart. You cannot repair things as they are; you must completely disassemble them. Do you understand? In the disassembly work, you must deny all the thoughts, powers, concepts, and positions you previously held. You must not acknowledge such things. Thus, you are completely disassembling. Does that feel unpleasant? Even if it feels unpleasant, it cannot be helped. If you do not do this, you cannot be repaired.

What should this disassembly work be centered around? Between the body and heart, the heart is somewhat better. Therefore, you leave the heart intact and completely tear apart the body. Thus, the truer the religion, the more it completely breaks down the body. The body’s desires are absolutely not tolerated. Only then can the heart become strong, and a person can live according to the heart's desires. Isn't that right? If one aspect becomes weak, the other aspect becomes strong, right? That is the kind of work we are doing. That is one method of repair.

What is the second method? People dislike it when the body is torn apart, right? Therefore, we leave the body alone and apply about ten times the strength to the heart. If the heart was at a 5 to 5 ratio with the body, injecting ten times the strength into the heart makes it 50 to 5. By injecting powerful strength into the heart, if a difference of about 10 to 1 occurs, the body can be led as desired.

Once you cross this threshold, if the heart leads the body for about three years, then even if you leave the heart alone, the body will not be able to go to bad places. If the body tries to go to bad places, it will feel pain as if its head is breaking or its legs will stick to the ground, making it impossible to move. This is what happens. This is what we call indemnity in the Unification Church. If you go to a bad place, your feelings will completely change. The body already knows.

Once the heart can go as it wishes, it will not be necessary to ask whether God exists or not. You will not be in a state of not knowing God. Did you do well to make God visible or not? You did well to make Him invisible. If God were visible, there would be a fight to seize God. The Soviet Union and the United States would fight to seize God from each other. Even so, God is not visible, but you are not in a state of not knowing Him.

The heart must govern the body for unity to occur. 

A person who truly loves does not seek to show it to others. They want to love quietly, without third-party intervention. There is a path for those who engage in true love. Therefore, we hold the invisible God deep within our hearts. It is good that God is not visible. So, what is the problem? The heart must be drawn down to a place where it can freely govern the body. To do this, strong power must be injected into the heart.

What is the method of injecting power into the heart? It is through prayer. When you pray earnestly, strength comes. When you strike the ground, it feels as if the ground breaks, and when you strike the heavens, it feels as if all the stars break apart. You can feel that the universe is playing in your embrace, and when you command, everything crumbles at your command. This is the powerful cosmic strength that emerges. At such times, when you hold a sick person and pray, miracles occur. In our Unification Church, if you make a resolution in your heart and just believe, you can heal without performing such wonders. Such power is at work.

So, what are we trying to achieve? Since the body and heart are divided, we aim to establish a unifying plan that will automatically lead us back to our original human position. Do you understand? Therefore, you must quickly carry out the disassembly work that you must do anyway. Whether you have been in the Unification Church for ten years or several decades, if you say you will not do this disassembly work or will only do it a little, you will not be able to do it even when the time comes to die.

Some will accomplish this within a month, some within a year, and some will attend church for their entire lives without doing this and will end up failing. Since it must be repaired anyway, those who quickly carry out the disassembly work are the wise ones. Do you understand? "Yes." You cannot do as you please.

We must once again realize that we are flawed beings and become the sons and daughters of the absolute being, united in purpose, so that we can eternally exist in the realm of God's love.
I ask that you become those who can live in a world so happy. This is the true path that life must take.

<Prayer> Beloved Father, please remember your children gathered here. Now they have embarked on the long journey of life, so may they not become those who drag themselves along from an unclear position where they have not fully clarified themselves, but rather may they become children who can live centered on You from a definitive and decisive position. I earnestly ask and wish that they may become sons and daughters who, by dismantling their currently insufficient selves and offering their completed forms before You, receive Your love without lacking anything.

I thank You for the grace of allowing us to gather today to share and hear Your words. Now, through this Masan region, I earnestly hope and wish that You will raise a new history of fire, and that Your sons and daughters will be able to fulfill their responsibilities within the eternal realm of Your love.

I am grateful for the grace of allowing such a time today. Until we meet again, may Your powerful hand be with them so that their lives and life journeys can be a light, and may they become Your children who fulfill the mission of pioneers of goodness, always able to remove evil in their daily lives.

This afternoon, Your children will be gathered in Busan waiting, so I ask that You bestow Your uniform grace upon that place as well, and may Your holy protection and love be with them on their way.

I earnestly ask that You grant uniform love to the family members who pray and care for this place. Thanking You for this time, I have offered all these words in the name of True Parents. Amen.
